<!-- ============================================================
  NOVYX — PART 5: CORE STATE, COINS, SAVE/LOAD,
                     SETTINGS & BACKGROUND LOGIC
  ============================================================ -->
<script>
// ── PERSISTENT STATE ─────────────────────────────────────────
var library       = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_library')    || '[]');
var recent        = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_recent')     || '[]');
var appliedBg     = localStorage.getItem('gv_bg')                    || 'default';
var currentUser   = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_user')       || 'null');
var stormCoins    = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('gv_coins')        || '100');
var ownedItems    = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_owned')      || '[]');
var equippedItems = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_equipped')   || '{}');
var lastFreeCoins = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('gv_last_free')    || '0');
var marketPrices  = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_market')     || 'null');

// Runtime-only
var searchQuery       = '';
var activeGenreFilter = 'All';
var plinkoAnimId      = null;
var cxRAF             = null;
var crashInterval     = null;

function saveState() {
  localStorage.setItem('gv_library',      JSON.stringify(library));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_recent',       JSON.stringify(recent));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_bg',           appliedBg);
  localStorage.setItem('gv_coins',        String(stormCoins));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_owned',        JSON.stringify(ownedItems));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_equipped',     JSON.stringify(equippedItems));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_last_free',    String(lastFreeCoins));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_market',       JSON.stringify(marketPrices));
}

// ── COINS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function updateCoins(delta) {
  // Apply streak XP multiplier to positive coin gains (not losses)
  var d = delta > 0 ? Math.round(delta * (_streakXP || 1.0)) : delta;
  stormCoins = Math.max(0, stormCoins + d);
  var delta = d;
  var fmt = stormCoins.toLocaleString();
  ['header-coins', 'casino-balance-hero'].forEach(function(id) {
    var e = document.getElementById(id); if (e) e.textContent = fmt;
  });
  var se = document.getElementById('shop-balance-display'); if (se) se.textContent = fmt;
  var sc = document.getElementById('stat-coins');           if (sc) sc.textContent = stormCoins;
  saveState();
}

// ── FREE COINS (every 2 hours) ─────────────────────────────────
var ONE_HOUR_MS = 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
function checkFreeCoinsBtn() {
  var now = Date.now(), elapsed = now - lastFreeCoins;
  var btn = document.getElementById('free-coins-btn');
  var timerEl = document.getElementById('free-coins-timer');
  if (!btn) return;
  if (elapsed >= ONE_HOUR_MS) {
    btn.className = 'casino-free-btn available';
    btn.textContent = '🎁 Claim 500 Free Storm Coins';
    btn.disabled = false;
    if (timerEl) timerEl.style.display = 'none';
  } else {
    var remaining = ONE_HOUR_MS - elapsed;
    var hrs  = Math.floor(remaining / 3600000);
    var mins = Math.floor((remaining % 3600000) / 60000);
    btn.className = 'casino-free-btn unavailable';
    btn.textContent = '⏳ Come back in ' + hrs + 'h ' + mins + 'm';
    btn.disabled = true;
    if (timerEl) { timerEl.style.display = 'block'; timerEl.textContent = 'Free coins every 2 hours.'; }
  }
}
function claimFreeCoins() {
  var now = Date.now();
  if (now - lastFreeCoins < ONE_HOUR_MS) { showToast('⏳ Already claimed! Come back in 2 hours.'); return; }
  lastFreeCoins = now;
  updateCoins(500);
  saveState();
  checkFreeCoinsBtn();
  showToast('🎁 +500 Storm Coins!');
  spawnParticles(['🎁', '⚡', '💰'], 12);
  addLiveBet('You', 'Free Coins', 0, 500);
}
setInterval(checkFreeCoinsBtn, 30000);

// ── SAVE / LOAD .GAMEV ────────────────────────────────────────
function saveGamevFile() {
  var data = {
    sig: 'GAMEV3', version: 3,
    savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    username: currentUser ? currentUser.username : 'unknown',
    createdAt: currentUser ? currentUser.createdAt : new Date().toISOString(),
    library: library, recent: recent,
    bg: appliedBg, customBg: localStorage.getItem('gv_custom_bg') || null,
    coins: stormCoins, owned: ownedItems, equipped: equippedItems,
    lastFreeCoins: lastFreeCoins, market: marketPrices
  };
  var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/octet-stream' });
  var url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  var a    = document.createElement('a');
  var uname = currentUser && currentUser.username ? currentUser.username : 'player';
  a.href     = url;
  a.download = 'novyx_' + uname.replace(/\s+/g, '_') + '_' + new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10) + '.gamev';
  document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); document.body.removeChild(a);
  setTimeout(function() { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 5000);
  showToast('💾 Saved!');
}
function triggerLoadGamev() { document.getElementById('gamev-file-input').click(); }
function loadGamevFile(input) {
  var file = input.files[0]; if (!file) return;
  if (!file.name.endsWith('.gamev')) { showToast('❌ Not a .gamev file'); input.value = ''; return; }
  var reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = function(e) {
    try {
      var data = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
      if (!data.sig || !data.sig.startsWith('GAMEV')) { showToast('❌ Invalid file'); return; }
      currentUser = { username: data.username || 'Player', createdAt: data.createdAt || new Date().toISOString() };
      localStorage.setItem('gv_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser));
      if (Array.isArray(data.library))  library  = data.library;
      if (Array.isArray(data.recent))   recent   = data.recent;
      if (data.bg) {
        appliedBg = data.bg;
        if (data.bg === 'custom' && data.customBg) localStorage.setItem('gv_custom_bg', data.customBg);
        restoreBackground();
      }
      if (data.coins   != null) stormCoins    = parseInt(data.coins) || 0;
      if (Array.isArray(data.owned))    ownedItems    = data.owned;
      if (data.equipped)                equippedItems = data.equipped;
      if (data.lastFreeCoins)           lastFreeCoins = parseInt(data.lastFreeCoins) || 0;
      if (data.market)                  marketPrices  = data.market;
      saveState(); reloadGames(); updateCoins(0); updateAccountBtn();
      renderDiscover(); renderLibrary(); renderRecent();
      renderCoinShop();
      document.getElementById('load-only-panel').style.display = 'none';
      showMainPanel(); checkFreeCoinsBtn();
      showToast('✅ Loaded!');
    } catch(err) { showToast('❌ Failed: ' + err.message); }
    input.value = '';
  };
  reader.readAsText(file);
}

// ── ACCOUNT MODAL ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function openAccountModal()  { document.getElementById('modal-backdrop').classList.add('open'); document.getElementById('account-modal').classList.add('open'); showCorrectPanel(); }
function closeAccountModal() { document.getElementById('modal-backdrop').classList.remove('open'); document.getElementById('account-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
function showCorrectPanel() {
  var hasUser = !!(currentUser && currentUser.username);
  document.getElementById('load-only-panel').style.display = hasUser ? 'none' : 'block';
  document.getElementById('main-panel').style.display      = hasUser ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (hasUser) showMainPanel();
}
function showMainPanel() {
  document.getElementById('main-panel').style.display      = 'block';
  document.getElementById('load-only-panel').style.display = 'none';
  var u = currentUser;
  document.getElementById('profile-big-avatar').textContent  = (u.username || '?')[0].toUpperCase();
  document.getElementById('profile-name-display').textContent = u.username;
  document.getElementById('profile-since').textContent = 'Since ' + new Date(u.createdAt).toLocaleDateString();
  document.getElementById('stat-library').textContent = library.length;
  document.getElementById('stat-played').textContent  = recent.length;
  document.getElementById('stat-coins').textContent   = stormCoins;
  applyEquippedFrame();
}
function setFreshUsername() {
  var val = document.getElementById('fresh-username').value.trim() || 'Player';
  currentUser = { username: val, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  localStorage.setItem('gv_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser));
  saveState(); updateAccountBtn(); showMainPanel();
  showToast('👾 Welcome, ' + val + '!');
}
function resetUsername() {
  currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('gv_user'); updateAccountBtn();
  document.getElementById('main-panel').style.display      = 'none';
  document.getElementById('load-only-panel').style.display = 'block';
}
function doLogout() {
  if (!confirm('Log out?')) return;
  currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('gv_user'); updateAccountBtn();
  closeAccountModal(); showToast('👋 Logged out!');
}
function updateAccountBtn() {
  var avatar = document.getElementById('account-avatar');
  var label  = document.getElementById('account-label');
  var btn    = document.getElementById('account-btn');
  if (currentUser && currentUser.username) {
    avatar.textContent = currentUser.username[0].toUpperCase();
    label.textContent  = currentUser.username;
    btn.classList.add('logged-in');
    applyEquippedFrame();
    var nb = document.getElementById('nav-level-badge');
    if (nb) nb.style.display = 'inline-flex';
    if (typeof updateRankStreakPill !== 'undefined') updateRankStreakPill();
  } else {
    avatar.textContent = '💾';
    label.textContent  = 'Save / Load';
    btn.classList.remove('logged-in');
  }
}
function applyEquippedFrame() {
  var avatar    = document.getElementById('account-avatar');
  var bigAvatar = document.getElementById('profile-big-avatar');
  var frameId   = equippedItems['frame'];
  [avatar, bigAvatar].forEach(function(el) {
    if (!el) return;
    el.className = el.id === 'account-avatar' ? 'account-avatar' : 'profile-big-avatar';
    if (frameId) el.classList.add(frameId);
  });
}

// ── PROFILE PICTURE ───────────────────────────────────────────
function settingsUploadPFP(input) {
  var file = input.files && input.files[0];
  if (!file) return;
  if (file.size > 2 * 1024 * 1024) { showToast('Image too large — max 2MB'); return; }
  var reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = function(ev) {
    var dataUrl = ev.target.result;
    localStorage.setItem('gv_avatar', dataUrl);
    applyAvatarToUI(dataUrl);
    showToast('✓ Profile picture updated', { icon: '📷' });
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
}

// ── SETTINGS: CHANGE DISPLAY NAME ────────────────────────────
function changeDisplayName() {
  var inp = document.getElementById('settings-username');
  if (!inp) return;
  var val = inp.value.trim();
  if (!val) { showToast('Enter a name first!'); return; }
  if (!currentUser) currentUser = { createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
  currentUser.username = val;
  localStorage.setItem('gv_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser));
  updateAccountBtn();
  showToast('✓ Display name updated to "' + val + '"!');
  inp.value = '';
}

// ── SETTINGS: RESET ALL DATA ──────────────────────────────────
function resetAllData() {
  library = []; recent = []; stormCoins = 0; ownedItems = []; equippedItems = {};
  marketPrices = null; lastFreeCoins = 0; appliedBg = 'default';
  currentUser = null;
  localStorage.clear();
  document.body.style.background = '';
  updateAccountBtn(); updateCoins(0);
  renderDiscover(); renderLibrary(); renderRecent();
  showToast('♻️ All data reset!');
}

function applyBackground(bg) {
  appliedBg = bg.id;
  localStorage.setItem('gv_bg', bg.id);
  localStorage.removeItem('gv_custom_bg');
  document.body.style.background = bg.css;
  renderBgGrids();
  var n = document.getElementById('custom-bg-name'); if (n) n.textContent = '';
  showToast('Background: ' + bg.name + ' ✓');
  saveState();
}

function applyUrlBackground() {
  var inp = document.getElementById('bg-url-input');
  if (!inp || !inp.value.trim()) { showToast('Enter a URL first!'); return; }
  var u = inp.value.trim();
  appliedBg = 'url-custom';
  localStorage.setItem('gv_bg', 'url-custom');
  localStorage.setItem('gv_custom_bg_url', u);
  document.body.style.backgroundImage      = 'url("' + u + '")';
  document.body.style.backgroundSize       = 'cover';
  document.body.style.backgroundPosition   = 'center';
  document.body.style.backgroundAttachment = 'fixed';
  document.body.style.backgroundRepeat     = 'no-repeat';
  var n = document.getElementById('custom-bg-name'); if (n) n.textContent = '✓ Custom URL applied';
  showToast('✓ Custom background applied!');
  saveState();
}

function resetBackground() {
  appliedBg = 'default';
  localStorage.setItem('gv_bg', 'default');
  localStorage.removeItem('gv_custom_bg');
  localStorage.removeItem('gv_custom_bg_url');
  document.body.style.background = '';
  document.body.style.backgroundImage = '';
  var n = document.getElementById('custom-bg-name'); if (n) n.textContent = '';
  var inp = document.getElementById('bg-url-input'); if (inp) inp.value = '';
  renderBgGrids();
  showToast('Background reset to default');
  saveState();
}

function restoreBackground() {
  if (!appliedBg || appliedBg === 'default') return;
  if (appliedBg === 'custom') {
    var d = localStorage.getItem('gv_custom_bg');
    if (d) { document.body.style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + d + ')'; document.body.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'; document.body.style.backgroundPosition = 'center'; document.body.style.backgroundAttachment = 'fixed'; }
    return;
  }
  if (appliedBg === 'url-custom') {
    var u = localStorage.getItem('gv_custom_bg_url');
    if (u) {
      document.body.style.backgroundImage      = 'url("' + u + '")';
      document.body.style.backgroundSize       = 'cover';
      document.body.style.backgroundPosition   = 'center';
      document.body.style.backgroundAttachment = 'fixed';
      document.body.style.backgroundRepeat     = 'no-repeat';
      var inp2 = document.getElementById('bg-url-input'); if (inp2) inp2.value = u;
    }
    return;
  }
  var all   = Object.values(backgrounds).flat();
  var found = all.find(function(b) { return b.id === appliedBg; });
  if (found) document.body.style.background = found.css;
}

function renderBgGrids() {
  Object.keys(backgrounds).forEach(function(category) {
    var grid = document.getElementById('bg-grid-' + category);
    if (!grid) return;
    grid.innerHTML = backgrounds[category].map(function(bg) {
      var isApplied = appliedBg === bg.id;
      var previewStyle = bg.css.startsWith('url(') || bg.css.startsWith('linear') || bg.css.startsWith('radial')
        ? 'background:' + bg.css + ';background-size:cover;background-position:center;'
        : 'background:' + bg.css + ';';
      return '<div class="bg-swatch' + (isApplied ? ' applied' : '') + '" onclick="applyBackground(' + JSON.stringify(bg).replace(/"/g,'&quot;') + ')">'
        + '<div class="bg-swatch-preview" style="' + previewStyle + '"></div>'
        + '<div class="bg-swatch-label"><div style="color:var(--text);font-weight:600">' + bg.name + '</div><div class="bg-swatch-tag">' + bg.tag + '</div></div>'
        + '</div>';
    }).join('');
  });
}
</script>
<!-- ============================================================
  NOVYX — PART 6: HERO BANNER, RENDER FUNCTIONS,
                     NAVIGATION & STARFIELD
  ============================================================ -->
<script>
// ── HERO CAROUSEL ─────────────────────────────────────────────
var heroPool  = BUILT_IN_GAMES.filter(function(g) { return !!heroImages[g.title]; });
var heroIndex = 0, heroTimer = null;
var heroTags  = ['🌟 Today\'s Pick', '🔥 Also Featured', '⭐ Daily Spotlight'];

function getDailyCarousel() {
  var pool  = heroPool.length >= 3 ? heroPool : BUILT_IN_GAMES;
  var day   = Math.floor((Date.now() - new Date(new Date().getFullYear(), 0, 0)) / 86400000);
  var gi    = day % Math.ceil(pool.length / 3), start = gi * 3;
  var slice = pool.slice(start, start + 3);
  if (slice.length < 3) slice = slice.concat(pool.slice(0, 3 - slice.length));
  return slice;
}
var carousel = getDailyCarousel();

function renderHero(instant) {
  var g = carousel[heroIndex];
  var img = document.getElementById('hero-img');
  var doUpdate = function() {
    img.src = heroImages[g.title] || g.img || ''; img.alt = g.title;
    document.getElementById('hero-title').textContent = g.title;
    document.getElementById('hero-desc').textContent  = g.genre + ' · ★ ' + g.rating;
    document.getElementById('hero-tag').textContent   = heroTags[heroIndex] || '🆕 Featured';
    var pb = document.getElementById('hero-play');
    pb.disabled   = !g.url;
    pb.textContent = g.url ? '▶ Play Now' : '🔒 Coming Soon';
    pb.onclick = function(e) { e.stopPropagation(); launchGame(g); };
    document.getElementById('hero-banner').onclick = function() { launchGame(g); };
    document.querySelectorAll('.hero-dot').forEach(function(d, i) { d.classList.toggle('active', i === heroIndex); });
    img.style.opacity = 1;
  };
  if (instant) { doUpdate(); return; }
  img.style.opacity = 0; setTimeout(doUpdate, 300);
}
function buildHeroDots() {
  var d = document.getElementById('hero-dots'); d.innerHTML = '';
  carousel.forEach(function(_, i) {
    var dot = document.createElement('div');
    dot.className = 'hero-dot' + (i === 0 ? ' active' : '');
    dot.onclick   = function(e) { e.stopPropagation(); heroIndex = i; renderHero(); resetHeroTimer(); };
    d.appendChild(dot);
  });
}
function heroStep(dir) { heroIndex = (heroIndex + dir + carousel.length) % carousel.length; renderHero(); resetHeroTimer(); }
function resetHeroTimer() {
  clearInterval(heroTimer);
  heroTimer = setInterval(function() { heroIndex = (heroIndex + 1) % carousel.length; renderHero(); }, 5000);
}
function initHero() { buildHeroDots(); renderHero(true); resetHeroTimer(); }

// ── GENRE FILTER ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function getAllGenres() {
  var genreSet = {};
  games.forEach(function(g) { genreSet[g.genre] = true; });
  return ['All'].concat(Object.keys(genreSet).sort());
}
function renderGenreFilter() {
  var el = document.getElementById('genre-filter-row'); if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = getAllGenres().map(function(g) {
    return '<div class="genre-pill' + (g === activeGenreFilter ? ' active' : '') + '" onclick="setGenreFilter(\'' + g + '\')">' + g + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}
function setGenreFilter(genre) { activeGenreFilter = genre; renderGenreFilter(); renderDiscover(); }

// ── DISCOVER GRID ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function renderDiscover() {
  var q    = searchQuery.toLowerCase();
  var list = games.filter(function(g) {
    var matchQuery = !q || (g.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) || g.genre.toLowerCase().includes(q));
    var matchGenre = activeGenreFilter === 'All' || g.genre === activeGenreFilter;
    return matchQuery && matchGenre;
  });
  var grid = document.getElementById('discover-grid'); grid.innerHTML = '';
  list.forEach(function(g, i) { grid.appendChild(makeCard(g, i * 20)); });
  // Inject enhancements
  setTimeout(function() { addSkeletonLoading(); injectCardRipples(); }, 50);

  var total    = games.length;
  var filtered = list.length;
  var countEl  = document.getElementById('discover-count');
  var bannerEl = document.getElementById('banner-game-count');
  if (bannerEl) bannerEl.textContent = total;
  if (filtered === total) {
    countEl.innerHTML = '<span style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.06);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1);border-radius:20px;padding:2px 10px;font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.45)">' + total + ' games</span>';
  } else {
    countEl.innerHTML = '<span style="background:rgba(99,102,241,0.12);border:1px solid rgba(99,102,241,0.3);border-radius:20px;padding:2px 10px;font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:#a5b4fc">' + filtered + ' / ' + total + '</span>';
  }
}

// ── LIBRARY ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
function renderLibrary() {
  var g = document.getElementById('library-grid'), e = document.getElementById('library-empty');
  g.innerHTML = '';
  if (!library.length) { e.style.display = 'flex'; }
  else { e.style.display = 'none'; library.forEach(function(g2, i) { g.appendChild(makeCard(g2, i * 20)); }); }
  document.getElementById('library-count').textContent = library.length ? library.length + ' games' : '';
}

// ── RECENT ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function renderRecent() {
  var l = document.getElementById('recent-list'), e = document.getElementById('recent-empty');
  if (!l) return;
  if (!recent.length) { e.style.display = 'flex'; }
  else {
    e.style.display = 'none';
    recent.forEach(function(g) {
      var ago = timeAgo(g.playedAt), row = document.createElement('div');
      row.className = 'recent-row';
      var gj = JSON.stringify(g).replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
      row.innerHTML = '<div class="recent-thumb">'
        + (g.img ? '<img src="' + g.img + '" alt="' + g.title + '" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">' : (g.emoji || '🎮'))
        + '</div>'
        + '<div class="recent-info"><div class="recent-title">' + g.title + '</div><div class="recent-meta">' + g.genre + ' · Played ' + ago + '</div></div>'
        + '<button class="recent-play"' + (g.url ? '' : ' disabled') + ' onclick="launchGame(' + gj + ')">' + (g.url ? '▶ Play' : 'N/A') + '</button>';
      l.appendChild(row);
    });
  }
  document.getElementById('recent-count').textContent = recent.length ? recent.length + ' games' : '';
}

// ── CARD FACTORY ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function makeCard(game, delay) {
  delay = delay || 0;
  var card     = document.createElement('div');
  card.className = 'game-card'; card.style.animationDelay = delay + 'ms';
  var coverHtml = game.img
    ? '<img class="card-img" src="' + game.img + '" alt="' + game.title + '" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\';this.nextElementSibling.style.display=\'flex\'">'
      + '<div class="card-placeholder" style="display:none"><div class="card-placeholder-icon">' + (game.emoji || '🎮') + '</div><div class="card-placeholder-name">' + game.title + '</div></div>'
    : '<div class="card-placeholder"><div class="card-placeholder-icon">' + (game.emoji || '🎮') + '</div><div class="card-placeholder-name">' + game.title + '</div></div>';
  var inLib  = isInLibrary(game);
  var hasUrl = !!game.url;
  var gj     = JSON.stringify(game).replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
  var badgeHtml = game.badge ? '<div class="card-badge" data-badge="' + game.badge + '">' + game.badge + '</div>' : '';
  card.innerHTML = badgeHtml
    + '<div class="card-inner">' + coverHtml
    + '<div class="card-body"><div class="card-title">' + game.title + '</div>'
    + '<div class="card-meta"><span class="card-genre">' + game.genre + '</span><span class="card-rating">★ ' + game.rating + '</span></div></div></div>'
    + '<div class="card-hover-overlay">'
    + '<button class="hover-btn hover-btn-play"' + (hasUrl ? '' : ' disabled') + ' onclick="event.stopPropagation();launchGame(' + gj + ')">' + (hasUrl ? '▶ Play Now' : '🔒 Coming Soon') + '</button>'
    + '<button class="hover-btn hover-btn-library' + (inLib ? ' in-library' : '') + '" onclick="event.stopPropagation();addToLibrary(' + gj + ',this)">' + (inLib ? '✓ In Library' : '+ Add to Library') + '</button>'
    + '</div>';
  return card;
}
function isInLibrary(game) { return !!library.find(function(g) { return g.title === game.title; }); }
function addToLibrary(game, btn) {
  if (library.find(function(g) { return g.title === game.title; })) {
    library = library.filter(function(g) { return g.title !== game.title; });
    showToast('Removed "' + game.title + '"');
  } else {
    library.push(game); showToast('Added "' + game.title + '" ✓');
    if (typeof checkAchievements === 'function') checkAchievements();
  }
  saveState(); renderLibrary(); renderDiscover();
  if (btn) {
    var inLib = !!library.find(function(g) { return g.title === game.title; });
    btn.className  = 'hover-btn hover-btn-library' + (inLib ? ' in-library' : '');
    btn.textContent = inLib ? '✓ In Library' : '+ Add to Library';
  }
}

// ── GAME LAUNCHER ─────────────────────────────────────────────
async function launchGame(game) {
  if (!game.url) return;
  recent = recent.filter(function(r) { return r.title !== game.title; });
  recent.unshift({ title: game.title, genre: game.genre, rating: game.rating, emoji: game.emoji, img: game.img || null, url: game.url, playedAt: Date.now() });
  if (recent.length > 20) recent = recent.slice(0, 20);
  saveState(); renderRecent();
  if (typeof trackAch !== 'undefined') trackAch('played', 0);
  if (typeof trackDC  !== 'undefined') {
    trackDC('plays', 1);
    if (game.genre && game.genre.toLowerCase().includes('horror')) trackDC('horror_play', 1);
  }
  if (typeof addXP !== 'undefined') addXP(5);
  if (typeof checkAchievements !== 'undefined') checkAchievements();

  // raw.githubusercontent.com serves HTML as plain text - must fetch & blob it
  if (game.url.includes('raw.githubusercontent.com')) {
    try {
      var res = await fetch(game.url);
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('HTTP ' + res.status);
      var html = await res.text();
      var blob = new Blob([html], { type: 'text/html' });
      var blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      var tab = window.open(blobUrl, '_blank');
      if (tab) setTimeout(function() { URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl); }, 10000);
    } catch(err) {
      window.open(game.url, '_blank');
    }
  } else {
    window.open(game.url, '_blank');
  }
}

// ── NAVIGATION ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function switchTab(tab) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.view').forEach(function(v)   { v.classList.remove('active'); });
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t)    { t.classList.remove('active'); });
  var view = document.getElementById('view-' + tab); if (view) view.classList.add('active');
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab="' + tab + '"]').forEach(function(el) { el.classList.add('active'); });
  if      (tab === 'discover')  { renderGenreFilter(); renderDiscover(); }
  else if (tab === 'library')   renderLibrary();
  else if (tab === 'store')     renderAchievements();
  else if (tab === 'settings')  { populateSettingsPage(); settingsTab(document.querySelector('.s-nav-btn'), 's-appearance'); }
  else if (tab === 'leaderboard') { /* AI helper - no init needed */; }
}
function onSearch(val) { searchQuery = val; renderDiscover(); }

// ── UTILITIES ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
function timeAgo(ts) {
  var s = Math.floor((Date.now() - ts) / 1000);
  if (s < 60)    return 'just now';
  if (s < 3600)  return Math.floor(s / 60)    + 'm ago';
  if (s < 86400) return Math.floor(s / 3600)  + 'h ago';
  return Math.floor(s / 86400) + 'd ago';
}
// ── TOAST — rich with icon, subtext, progress bar ─────────────
var _toastQueue = [], _toastActive = false;

function showToast(msg, opts) {
  // opts: { sub, type ('win'|'lose'|'info'|'coin'), icon, duration }
  _toastQueue.push({ msg: msg, opts: opts || {} });
  if (!_toastActive) _processToastQueue();
}

function _processToastQueue() {
  if (!_toastQueue.length) { _toastActive = false; return; }
  _toastActive = true;
  var item = _toastQueue.shift();
  var msg = item.msg, opts = item.opts;
  var t    = document.getElementById('toast');
  var ico  = document.getElementById('toast-icon');
  var ttl  = document.getElementById('toast-title');
  var sub  = document.getElementById('toast-sub');
  var bar  = document.getElementById('toast-progress');
  if (!t) return;

  // Auto-detect icon from message
  var icon = opts.icon || '';
  if (!icon) {
    if      (msg.includes('WIN') || msg.includes('won') || msg.includes('Claimed'))  icon = '🏆';
    else if (msg.includes('Saved') || msg.includes('💾'))   icon = '💾';
    else if (msg.includes('Loaded') || msg.includes('✅'))  icon = '✅';
    else if (msg.includes('Coins') || msg.includes('⚡'))   icon = '⚡';
    else if (msg.includes('❌') || msg.includes('Lost'))    icon = '❌';
    else if (msg.includes('Cleared') || msg.includes('✓')) icon = '✓';
    else if (msg.includes('Welcome') || msg.includes('👾')) icon = '👾';
    else icon = '💬';
  }

  // Auto-detect type
  var type = opts.type || '';
  if (!type) {
    if      (msg.includes('WIN') || msg.includes('+⚡') || msg.includes('JACKPOT'))  type = 't-win';
    else if (msg.includes('Lost') || msg.includes('Boom') || msg.includes('SPLAT'))  type = 't-lose';
    else if (msg.includes('⚡') && (msg.includes('Coins') || msg.includes('Claim'))) type = 't-coin';
    else type = 't-info';
  }

  ico.textContent  = icon;
  ttl.textContent  = msg.replace(/^[^\w\s🎮🎁💾📂✅❌👾⚡🏆🃏🎰🎲🪙🎡🚀💣💎🔫🎯]+\s*/, '');
  ttl.textContent  = msg;
  if (opts.sub) { sub.textContent = opts.sub; sub.style.display = 'block'; }
  else { sub.style.display = 'none'; }

  t.className = 'toast ' + type;
  var dur = opts.duration || 3000;

  // Progress bar
  if (bar) {
    bar.style.transition = 'none';
    bar.style.width = '100%';
    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
      requestAnimationFrame(function() {
        bar.style.transition = 'width ' + dur + 'ms linear';
        bar.style.width = '0%';
      });
    });
  }

  t.classList.add('show');
  clearTimeout(t._timer);
  t._timer = setTimeout(function() {
    t.classList.remove('show');
    setTimeout(_processToastQueue, 340);
  }, dur);
}

// ── COIN BUMP ANIMATION ───────────────────────────────────────
function bumpCoins() {
  var el = document.getElementById('header-coins');
  if (!el) return;
  el.classList.remove('coin-bump');
  void el.offsetWidth; // reflow
  el.classList.add('coin-bump');
  setTimeout(function() { el.classList.remove('coin-bump'); }, 400);
}

// ── COIN RAIN ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
function spawnCoinRain(count) {
  count = count || 18;
  for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    (function(idx) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        var p = document.createElement('div');
        p.className = 'coin-rain';
        p.textContent = ['⚡','💰','🪙','💎'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
        p.style.left  = (5 + Math.random() * 90) + '%';
        p.style.top   = '-30px';
        p.style.fontSize = (14 + Math.random() * 10) + 'px';
        p.style.animationDuration = (1.4 + Math.random() * 1) + 's';
        p.style.animationDelay    = (Math.random() * 0.3) + 's';
        document.body.appendChild(p);
        setTimeout(function() { p.remove(); }, 2800);
      }, idx * 55);
    })(i);
  }
}

// ── ENHANCED PARTICLES ────────────────────────────────────────
function spawnParticles(icons, count) {
  for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    (function(idx) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        var p = document.createElement('div');
        p.className = 'win-particle';
        p.textContent = icons[Math.floor(Math.random() * icons.length)];
        var x = 15 + Math.random() * 70;
        var y = 30 + Math.random() * 40;
        var dir = Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
        p.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;z-index:9998;font-size:' + (18 + Math.random() * 14) + 'px;left:' + x + '%;top:' + y + '%;pointer-events:none;animation:particleFly 1.5s ease forwards;';
        document.body.appendChild(p);
        setTimeout(function() { p.remove(); }, 1700);
      }, idx * 65);
    })(i);
  }
}

// ── RIPPLE ON CARD CLICK ──────────────────────────────────────
function addRipple(el, e) {
  var rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
  var size = Math.max(rect.width, rect.height) * 0.6;
  var x = (e.clientX - rect.left) - size / 2;
  var y = (e.clientY - rect.top)  - size / 2;
  var ripple = document.createElement('span');
  ripple.className = 'ripple';
  ripple.style.cssText = 'width:' + size + 'px;height:' + size + 'px;left:' + x + 'px;top:' + y + 'px;';
  el.appendChild(ripple);
  setTimeout(function() { ripple.remove(); }, 600);
}

// ── SCROLL TO TOP ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function scrollActiveViewTop() {
  window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
}
function initScrollTopBtn() {
  var btn = document.getElementById('scroll-top-btn');
  window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('visible', window.scrollY > 200);
  });
}

// ── KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS ────────────────────────────────────────
function initKeyboardShortcuts() {
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    // Don't fire when typing in an input
    var tag = document.activeElement ? document.activeElement.tagName : '';
    if (tag === 'INPUT' || tag === 'TEXTAREA' || tag === 'SELECT') return;

    switch (e.key) {
      case '1': switchTab('discover'); break;
      case '2': switchTab('library'); break;
      case '4': switchTab('store'); break;
      case '5': switchTab('casino'); break;

      case '7': switchTab('settings'); break;

      case '/':
      case 'f':
        e.preventDefault();
        var s = document.getElementById('search-input');
        if (s) { s.focus(); switchTab('discover'); }
        break;
      case 'Escape':
        var si = document.getElementById('search-input');
        if (si && si.value) { si.value = ''; onSearch(''); }
        closeCasinoGame && closeCasinoGame();
        closeAccountModal && closeAccountModal();
        break;
      case 't':
      case 'T':
        scrollActiveViewTop();
        break;
    }
  });
}

// ── STAT COUNTER ANIMATION ────────────────────────────────────
function animateCount(el, from, to, duration) {
  var start = null;
  var step = function(ts) {
    if (!start) start = ts;
    var progress = Math.min((ts - start) / duration, 1);
    var ease = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
    el.textContent = Math.floor(from + (to - from) * ease).toLocaleString();
    if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(step);
  };
  requestAnimationFrame(step);
}

// ── CARD RIPPLE INJECTION ─────────────────────────────────────
function injectCardRipples() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.game-card .card-inner').forEach(function(inner) {
    if (inner._hasRipple) return;
    inner._hasRipple = true;
    inner.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    inner.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) { addRipple(inner, e); });
  });
}

// ── DISCOVER: search highlight in card titles ─────────────────
function highlightTitle(title, query) {
  if (!query) return title;
  var idx = title.toLowerCase().indexOf(query.toLowerCase());
  if (idx === -1) return title;
  return title.slice(0, idx)
    + '<span class="search-hl">' + title.slice(idx, idx + query.length) + '</span>'
    + title.slice(idx + query.length);
}

// ── IMAGE SKELETON LOADING ────────────────────────────────────
function addSkeletonLoading() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.card-img').forEach(function(img) {
    if (img._skelDone) return;
    img._skelDone = true;
    if (!img.complete) {
      img.classList.add('card-img-loading');
      img.addEventListener('load',  function() { img.classList.remove('card-img-loading'); });
      img.addEventListener('error', function() { img.classList.remove('card-img-loading'); });
    }
  });
}

// Observe new cards added to DOM
var _cardObserver = new MutationObserver(function() {
  addSkeletonLoading();
  injectCardRipples();
});
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  var grids = document.querySelectorAll('.cards-grid, .casino-games-grid');
  grids.forEach(function(g) {
    _cardObserver.observe(g, { childList: true });
  });
});

// ── INIT ALL ENHANCEMENTS ─────────────────────────────────────
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  initScrollTopBtn();
  initKeyboardShortcuts();
});

function runHtmlViewer() {
  var src = document.getElementById('html-input').value;
  if (!src.trim()) { showToast('Enter HTML first'); return; }
  var f  = document.getElementById('html-preview');
  var ph = document.getElementById('html-placeholder');
  if (ph) ph.style.display = 'none';
  try { f.srcdoc = src; } catch(e) { showToast('Invalid HTML'); }
}
function clearHtmlViewer() {
  document.getElementById('html-input').value = '';
  document.getElementById('html-preview').srcdoc = '';
  var ph = document.getElementById('html-placeholder'); if (ph) ph.style.display = '';
}

// ── STARFIELD ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
function initStarfield() {
  var canvas = document.getElementById('starfield');
  if (!canvas) return;
  var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

  function resize() {
    canvas.width  = window.innerWidth;
    canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
  }
  resize();
  window.addEventListener('resize', function() { resize(); initParticles(); });

  var tiny = [], mid = [], big = [], shoots = [], nebulas = [];

  function initParticles() {
    var W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;
    tiny = []; mid = []; big = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < 320; i++) {
      tiny.push({ x:Math.random()*W, y:Math.random()*H, r:Math.random()*0.8+0.2, alpha:Math.random()*0.5+0.05,
        twinkleSpeed:Math.random()*0.03+0.008, twinkleAmp:Math.random()*0.3+0.05,
        phase:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, color:Math.random()<0.15?'b':Math.random()<0.1?'r':'w' });
    }
    for (var i = 0; i < 90; i++) {
      mid.push({ x:Math.random()*W, y:Math.random()*H, r:Math.random()*1.4+0.6, alpha:Math.random()*0.55+0.15,
        twinkleSpeed:Math.random()*0.025+0.005, twinkleAmp:Math.random()*0.35+0.1,
        phase:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, driftX:(Math.random()-0.5)*0.04, driftY:(Math.random()-0.5)*0.015,
        color:Math.random()<0.2?'b':Math.random()<0.1?'y':'w' });
    }
    for (var i = 0; i < 28; i++) {
      big.push({ x:Math.random()*W, y:Math.random()*H, r:Math.random()*1.8+1.4, alpha:Math.random()*0.6+0.3,
        twinkleSpeed:Math.random()*0.018+0.004, twinkleAmp:Math.random()*0.4+0.15,
        phase:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, driftX:(Math.random()-0.5)*0.025, driftY:(Math.random()-0.5)*0.01,
        crossLen:Math.random()*8+5, color:Math.random()<0.25?'b':Math.random()<0.15?'y':'w' });
    }
    nebulas = [
      { x:W*0.12, y:H*0.28, rx:W*0.22, ry:H*0.35, c:[75,45,160],  a:0.055 },
      { x:W*0.8,  y:H*0.65, rx:W*0.26, ry:H*0.40, c:[40,65,185],  a:0.04  },
      { x:W*0.5,  y:H*0.08, rx:W*0.20, ry:H*0.28, c:[95,40,175],  a:0.038 },
      { x:W*0.35, y:H*0.85, rx:W*0.18, ry:H*0.22, c:[30,80,160],  a:0.028 },
      { x:W*0.92, y:H*0.18, rx:W*0.14, ry:H*0.20, c:[120,40,150], a:0.032 }
    ];
  }

  function spawnShoot() {
    var W=canvas.width,H=canvas.height;
    var angle=(Math.random()*30+10)*Math.PI/180;
    var startX=Math.random()*W*1.2-W*0.1,startY=Math.random()*H*0.5;
    var speed=Math.random()*5+6;
    shoots.push({ x:startX,y:startY,vx:Math.cos(angle)*speed,vy:Math.sin(angle)*speed,
      len:Math.random()*120+60,alpha:0,life:0,maxLife:Math.random()*60+50,r:Math.random()*0.8+0.4 });
  }

  function colorFor(type,alpha) {
    if(type==='b')return 'rgba(160,190,255,'+alpha+')';
    if(type==='r')return 'rgba(255,180,160,'+alpha+')';
    if(type==='y')return 'rgba(255,240,180,'+alpha+')';
    return 'rgba(215,220,255,'+alpha+')';
  }

  initParticles();
  for(var i=0;i<2;i++) setTimeout(spawnShoot,i*2000+Math.random()*3000);
  setInterval(function(){if(Math.random()<0.6)spawnShoot();},3500);

  var t=0,mx=0,my=0;
  document.addEventListener('mousemove',function(e){mx=e.clientX;my=e.clientY;});

  function draw() {
    var W=canvas.width,H=canvas.height;
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);ctx.fillStyle='#08090f';ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    // Nebulas
    nebulas.forEach(function(n){
      if(!n.rx||!n.ry||!isFinite(n.rx)||!isFinite(n.ry)||n.rx<=0||n.ry<=0)return;
      ctx.save();ctx.scale(1,n.ry/n.rx);
      var gy=n.y*n.rx/n.ry;
      if(!isFinite(gy)||!isFinite(n.x)||!isFinite(n.rx))return ctx.restore();
      var g=ctx.createRadialGradient(n.x,gy,0,n.x,gy,n.rx);
      g.addColorStop(0,'rgba('+n.c[0]+','+n.c[1]+','+n.c[2]+','+n.a+')');
      g.addColorStop(0.5,'rgba('+n.c[0]+','+n.c[1]+','+n.c[2]+','+(n.a*0.4)+')');
      g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');ctx.fillStyle=g;
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(n.x,gy,n.rx,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();ctx.restore();
    });
    // Tiny stars
    tiny.forEach(function(s){
      var a=Math.max(0,s.alpha+Math.sin(t*s.twinkleSpeed+s.phase)*s.twinkleAmp);
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(s.x,s.y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=colorFor(s.color,a);ctx.fill();
    });
    // Mid stars with parallax
    var px=(mx/W-0.5)*6,py=(my/H-0.5)*3;
    mid.forEach(function(s){
      s.x+=s.driftX;s.y+=s.driftY;
      if(s.x<-2)s.x=W+2;if(s.x>W+2)s.x=-2;if(s.y<-2)s.y=H+2;if(s.y>H+2)s.y=-2;
      var a=Math.max(0,s.alpha+Math.sin(t*s.twinkleSpeed+s.phase)*s.twinkleAmp);
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(s.x+px*0.3,s.y+py*0.15,s.r,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=colorFor(s.color,a);ctx.fill();
    });
    // Big stars with cross sparkle
    big.forEach(function(s){
      s.x+=s.driftX;s.y+=s.driftY;
      if(s.x<-3)s.x=W+3;if(s.x>W+3)s.x=-3;if(s.y<-3)s.y=H+3;if(s.y>H+3)s.y=-3;
      var a=Math.max(0,Math.min(1,s.alpha+Math.sin(t*s.twinkleSpeed+s.phase)*s.twinkleAmp));
      var cx2=s.x+px*0.6,cy2=s.y+py*0.3;
      if(!isFinite(cx2)||!isFinite(cy2)||!isFinite(s.r)||s.r<=0)return;
      var grd=ctx.createRadialGradient(cx2,cy2,0,cx2,cy2,s.r*3);
      grd.addColorStop(0,colorFor(s.color,a));grd.addColorStop(0.4,colorFor(s.color,a*0.4));grd.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(cx2,cy2,s.r*3,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=grd;ctx.fill();
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(cx2,cy2,s.r,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=colorFor(s.color,Math.min(1,a*1.3));ctx.fill();
      var cl=s.crossLen*(0.7+Math.sin(t*s.twinkleSpeed*1.5+s.phase)*0.3),ca=a*0.5;
      if(!isFinite(cl)||cl<=0)return;
      var gH=ctx.createLinearGradient(cx2-cl,cy2,cx2+cl,cy2);
      gH.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');gH.addColorStop(0.5,colorFor(s.color,ca));gH.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.strokeStyle=gH;ctx.lineWidth=0.6;
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(cx2-cl,cy2);ctx.lineTo(cx2+cl,cy2);ctx.stroke();
      var gV=ctx.createLinearGradient(cx2,cy2-cl,cx2,cy2+cl);
      gV.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');gV.addColorStop(0.5,colorFor(s.color,ca));gV.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.strokeStyle=gV;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(cx2,cy2-cl);ctx.lineTo(cx2,cy2+cl);ctx.stroke();
    });
    // Shooting stars
    shoots=shoots.filter(function(s){return s.life<s.maxLife;});
    shoots.forEach(function(s){
      s.life++;s.x+=s.vx;s.y+=s.vy;
      var progress=s.life/s.maxLife;
      s.alpha=progress<0.2?progress/0.2:progress>0.7?(1-progress)/0.3:1;
      var spd=Math.sqrt(s.vx*s.vx+s.vy*s.vy);
      if(!spd||!isFinite(spd))return;
      var tailX=s.x-s.vx*(s.len/spd),tailY=s.y-s.vy*(s.len/spd);
      if(!isFinite(tailX)||!isFinite(tailY))return;
      var sg=ctx.createLinearGradient(tailX,tailY,s.x,s.y);
      sg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,255,255,0)');sg.addColorStop(0.6,'rgba(200,210,255,'+(s.alpha*0.4)+')');sg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(255,255,255,'+s.alpha+')');
      ctx.strokeStyle=sg;ctx.lineWidth=s.r;ctx.lineCap='round';
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(tailX,tailY);ctx.lineTo(s.x,s.y);ctx.stroke();
      if(isFinite(s.r)&&s.r>0){ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(s.x,s.y,s.r*1.5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,'+s.alpha+')';ctx.fill();}
    });
    t+=0.012;
    requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  }
  draw();
}

// ── SETTINGS PAGE POPULATE ────────────────────────────────────
function settingsTab(btn, id) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.s-nav-btn').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('active'); });
  document.querySelectorAll('.s-section').forEach(function(s){ s.style.display = 'none'; });
  btn.classList.add('active');
  var sec = document.getElementById(id);
  if (sec) sec.style.display = 'block';
}

function populateSettingsPage() {
  var cu = document.getElementById('settings-current-user');
  if (cu) cu.textContent = (currentUser && currentUser.username) ? currentUser.username : 'Not logged in';
  var gc = document.getElementById('settings-game-count');
  if (gc) gc.textContent = games.length + ' games';
  var lc = document.getElementById('settings-lib-count');
  if (lc) lc.textContent = library.length + ' game' + (library.length !== 1 ? 's' : '');
  var cc = document.getElementById('settings-coin-count');
  if (cc) cc.textContent = '\u26A1' + stormCoins.toLocaleString();
  var ld = document.getElementById('settings-level-display');
  if (ld && typeof getLevel !== 'undefined') { var lv=getLevel(); ld.textContent=lv.emoji+' '+lv.name; }
  var sd = document.getElementById('settings-streak-display');
  if (sd) sd.textContent = (_streak||0) + ' day' + ((_streak||0)!==1?'s':'');
  var ap = document.getElementById('settings-avatar-preview');
  if (ap) {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('gv_avatar');
    if (saved && saved.startsWith('data:')) {
      ap.innerHTML = '<img src="'+saved+'" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;border-radius:12px;">';
    } else {
      ap.textContent = currentUser && currentUser.username ? currentUser.username[0].toUpperCase() : '?';
    }
  }
  if (typeof buildSettingsThemeSwatches === 'function') buildSettingsThemeSwatches();
  buildAccentSwatches();
  renderPanicKeyStatus();
  loadQuickNotes();
}

// ── ACCENT COLOR ──────────────────────────────────────────────
var ACCENT_PRESETS = [
  { name:'Purple',  a:'#7c3aed', b:'#a855f7' },
  { name:'Blue',    a:'#1d4ed8', b:'#3b82f6' },
  { name:'Cyan',    a:'#0891b2', b:'#22d3ee' },
  { name:'Green',   a:'#059669', b:'#4ade80' },
  { name:'Rose',    a:'#be123c', b:'#fb7185' },
  { name:'Orange',  a:'#c2410c', b:'#fb923c' },
  { name:'Pink',    a:'#9d174d', b:'#f472b6' },
  { name:'Indigo',  a:'#3730a3', b:'#818cf8' },
  { name:'Teal',    a:'#0f766e', b:'#2dd4bf' },
  { name:'Yellow',  a:'#a16207', b:'#facc15' },
  { name:'Red',     a:'#991b1b', b:'#f87171' },
  { name:'White',   a:'#475569', b:'#cbd5e1' },
];

function buildAccentSwatches() {
  var grid = document.getElementById('accent-swatches');
  if (!grid) return;
  var saved = localStorage.getItem('gv_accent_preset') || 'Purple';
  grid.innerHTML = ACCENT_PRESETS.map(function(p) {
    var active = saved === p.name;
    return '<div onclick="applyAccentPreset(\'' + p.name + '\',\'' + p.a + '\',\'' + p.b + '\')" title="' + p.name + '" style="'
      + 'display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:6px;cursor:pointer;'
      + 'padding:8px 4px;border-radius:12px;'
      + 'border:1px solid ' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)') + ';'
      + 'background:' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)' : 'transparent') + ';'
      + 'transition:all 0.15s;"'
      + ' onmouseover="this.style.background=\'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)\'"'
      + ' onmouseout="this.style.background=\'' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)' : 'transparent') + '\'">'
      + '<div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:50%;'
      + 'background:linear-gradient(135deg,' + p.a + ',' + p.b + ');'
      + 'box-shadow:' + (active ? '0 0 12px ' + p.b + '99,0 0 0 2px rgba(255,255,255,0.3)' : '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.4)') + ';'
      + 'flex-shrink:0;position:relative;">'
      + (active ? '<div style="position:absolute;inset:0;border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:14px;">✓</div>' : '')
      + '</div>'
      + '<span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:600;color:' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.8)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.3)') + ';letter-spacing:0.3px;text-align:center;line-height:1;">' + p.name + '</span>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function applyAccentPreset(name, a, b) {
  localStorage.setItem('gv_accent_preset', name);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', a);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent2', b);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a', a);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a2', b);
  localStorage.setItem('gv_accent_custom', JSON.stringify({ a:a, b:b }));
  buildAccentSwatches();
  showToast('🎨 ' + name + ' accent applied');
}

function applyCustomAccent(hex) {
  function lighten(h, amt) {
    var r=parseInt(h.slice(1,3),16), g=parseInt(h.slice(3,5),16), b=parseInt(h.slice(5,7),16);
    r=Math.min(255,r+amt); g=Math.min(255,g+amt); b=Math.min(255,b+amt);
    return '#'+[r,g,b].map(function(x){return x.toString(16).padStart(2,'0');}).join('');
  }
  var lighter = lighten(hex, 40);
  localStorage.setItem('gv_accent_preset', 'custom');
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', hex);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent2', lighter);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a', hex);
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a2', lighter);
  localStorage.setItem('gv_accent_custom', JSON.stringify({ a:hex, b:lighter }));
  buildAccentSwatches();
}

function resetAccentColor() {
  localStorage.removeItem('gv_accent_custom');
  localStorage.setItem('gv_accent_preset', 'Purple');
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', '#7c3aed');
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent2', '#a855f7');
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a', '#7c3aed');
  document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a2', '#a855f7');
  buildAccentSwatches();
  showToast('🎨 Accent reset to purple');
}

function restoreAccentColor() {
  var saved = localStorage.getItem('gv_accent_custom');
  if (saved) {
    try {
      var c = JSON.parse(saved);
      document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', c.a);
      document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent2', c.b);
      document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a', c.a);
      document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--nav-ring-a2', c.b);
    } catch(e) {}
  }
}

// ── PANIC KEY ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
var _panicKey       = localStorage.getItem('gv_panic_key') || '';
var _capturingPanic = false;

function startPanicKeyCapture() {
  var disp = document.getElementById('panic-key-display');
  if (!disp) return;
  _capturingPanic = true;
  disp.textContent = 'Press any key…';
  disp.style.borderColor = 'rgba(245,158,11,0.6)';
  disp.style.color = '#f59e0b';
}

function renderPanicKeyStatus() {
  var disp = document.getElementById('panic-key-display');
  var stat = document.getElementById('panic-key-status');
  if (disp) disp.textContent = _panicKey ? 'Key: ' + _panicKey.toUpperCase() : 'Click to set key…';
  if (stat) stat.textContent = _panicKey ? '✓ Panic key active — press ' + _panicKey.toUpperCase() + ' anywhere to escape' : 'No panic key set';
  renderPanicUrlInput();
}

var _panicUrl = localStorage.getItem('gv_panic_url') || '';

function savePanicUrl() {
  var inp = document.getElementById('panic-url-input');
  if (!inp) return;
  var val = inp.value.trim();
  if (val && !val.startsWith('http')) val = 'https://' + val;
  _panicUrl = val || '';
  if (_panicUrl) {
    localStorage.setItem('gv_panic_url', _panicUrl);
    showToast('🚨 Redirect URL saved');
  } else {
    localStorage.removeItem('gv_panic_url');
    showToast('Redirect URL cleared — will use Google');
  }
  renderPanicKeyStatus();
}

function renderPanicUrlInput() {
  var inp = document.getElementById('panic-url-input');
  var stat = document.getElementById('panic-url-status');
  if (inp) inp.value = _panicUrl || '';
  if (stat) stat.textContent = _panicUrl ? '✓ Will redirect to: ' + _panicUrl : 'No custom URL — defaults to google.com';
}

function clearPanicKey() {
  _panicKey = '';
  localStorage.removeItem('gv_panic_key');
  renderPanicKeyStatus();
  showToast('Panic key cleared');
}

document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
  // Capture mode
  if (_capturingPanic) {
    _capturingPanic = false;
    var key = e.key;
    if (key === 'Escape' || key === 'Enter') { renderPanicKeyStatus(); return; }
    _panicKey = key;
    localStorage.setItem('gv_panic_key', key);
    renderPanicKeyStatus();
    var disp = document.getElementById('panic-key-display');
    if (disp) { disp.style.borderColor = ''; disp.style.color = ''; }
    showToast('🚨 Panic key set to ' + key.toUpperCase());
    e.preventDefault(); return;
  }
  // Panic mode — trigger if key matches and not in an input
  if (_panicKey && e.key === _panicKey) {
    var tag = document.activeElement ? document.activeElement.tagName : '';
    if (tag === 'INPUT' || tag === 'TEXTAREA' || tag === 'SELECT') return;
    // Open Google in current tab, try to close (works if opened by script)
    var dest = _panicUrl || 'https://www.google.com';
    try { window.open(dest,'_self'); } catch(e) {}
    try { window.close(); } catch(e) {}
  }
});

// ── WIN SOUNDS ────────────────────────────────────────────────
var _winSoundOn  = localStorage.getItem('gv_win_sound') === 'true';
var _audioCtx    = null;

function getAudioCtx() {
  if (!_audioCtx) {
    try { _audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)(); } catch(e) {}
  }
  return _audioCtx;
}

function playTone(freqs, duration, type, vol) {
  var ctx = getAudioCtx();
  if (!ctx) return;
  freqs.forEach(function(f, i) {
    var osc  = ctx.createOscillator();
    var gain = ctx.createGain();
    osc.connect(gain); gain.connect(ctx.destination);
    osc.type = type || 'sine';
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(f, ctx.currentTime + i * 0.08);
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(vol || 0.18, ctx.currentTime + i * 0.08);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ctx.currentTime + i * 0.08 + duration);
    osc.start(ctx.currentTime + i * 0.08);
    osc.stop(ctx.currentTime + i * 0.08 + duration + 0.05);
  });
}

function previewWinSound(){}
function toggleWinSound(){}
function renderWinSoundToggle(){}

function playWinSound(isBig) {
  if (!_winSoundOn) return;
  if (isBig) playTone([523,659,784,1047], 0.25, 'triangle', 0.22);
  else       playTone([523,659,784], 0.18, 'sine', 0.2);
}

function playLossSound() {
  if (!_winSoundOn) return;
  playTone([220,196], 0.3, 'sawtooth', 0.1);
}

function toggleWinSound(on) {
  _winSoundOn = on;
  localStorage.setItem('gv_win_sound', on ? 'true' : 'false');
  
  if (on) previewWinSound('win');
}

function renderWinSoundToggle() {
  var cb    = document.getElementById('win-sound-toggle');
  var track = document.getElementById('win-sound-track');
  var thumb = document.getElementById('win-sound-thumb');
  if (cb)    cb.checked = _winSoundOn;
  if (track) track.style.background = _winSoundOn ? 'var(--accent)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)';
  if (thumb) thumb.style.transform  = _winSoundOn ? 'translateX(20px)' : 'translateX(0)';
  if (thumb) thumb.style.background = _winSoundOn ? '#fff' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)';
}

// ── DISCOVER LIVE PLAYERS COUNTER (max 15, realistic) ─────────
var _discoverPlayers = (function() {
  var current = 7 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 9); // start 7-15
  var target  = current;

  function render() {
    var el = document.getElementById('discover-player-count');
    if (el) el.textContent = current;
  }

  function tick() {
    if      (current < target) current++;
    else if (current > target) current--;
    render();
  }

  function setNewTarget() {
    target = 7 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 9); // always 7-15
  }

  setNewTarget();
  return {
    init: function() {
      render();
      setInterval(tick, 3000);
      setInterval(setNewTarget, 20000);
    }
  };
})();

}

// ── NAV INIT ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
function initNav() {
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-tab]').forEach(function(el) {
    el.addEventListener('click', function() { switchTab(el.dataset.tab); });
  });
  initStarfield();
  restoreBackground(); checkFreeCoinsBtn(); /* hero removed */
  if (currentUser) showMainPanel();
  renderGenreFilter(); renderDiscover(); renderLibrary(); renderRecent(); updateCoins(0);
  startSettingsOnlineCounter();

  // Live bets feed
  var betNames = ['Lucky','King','Storm','Ace','Bolt','Flash','Nova','Zap','Viper','Ghost'];
  var betGames = ['Slots','Crash','Roulette','Blackjack','Dice','Plinko','Coin Flip','Hi-Lo','CS Cases','Mines','Poker','Baccarat','Crossy Road'];
  function addRandBet() {
    var u = betNames[Math.floor(Math.random() * betNames.length)];
    var g = betGames[Math.floor(Math.random() * betGames.length)];
    var amt = [10,25,50,100,200][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
    var win = Math.random() > 0.48;
    var profit = win ? amt * (1 + Math.random() * 2) : amt;
    addLiveBet(u, g, amt, win ? profit : -profit);
  }
  setInterval(addRandBet, 2800);
  setInterval(function() {
    var oc = document.getElementById('online-count');
    if (oc) oc.textContent = (7 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 9)).toString();
  }, 6000);
}

<script>
// ── MARKET ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
var BASE_PRICES = {
  'frame-gold':8000,'frame-neon':5000,'frame-fire':7500,'frame-galaxy':12000,
  'frame-emerald':6000,'frame-diamond':18000,'badge-whale':3500,'badge-lucky':2500,
  'badge-skull':5000,'badge-storm':9000,'badge-jackpot':7000,'badge-robot':1800,
  'fx-confetti':3500,'fx-lightning':6000,'fx-fire-win':9000,'fx-coins':5000,
  'legendary-godframe':200000
};
function initMarket() {
  if (!marketPrices) {
    marketPrices = {};
    for (var id in BASE_PRICES) {
      marketPrices[id] = { price: BASE_PRICES[id], lastUpdate: Date.now(), trend: Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1, prevPrice: BASE_PRICES[id] };
    }
  }
  var now = Date.now();
  for (var id in marketPrices) {
    var entry = marketPrices[id]; var age = (now - entry.lastUpdate) / 3600000;
    if (age > 1) {
      var base = BASE_PRICES[id] || entry.price;
      var change = (Math.random() * 0.3 - 0.1) * entry.trend;
      var newPrice = Math.round(base * (1 + change));
      newPrice = Math.max(Math.round(base * 0.5), Math.min(Math.round(base * 2.5), newPrice));
      entry.trend = Math.random() > 0.4 ? 1 : -1;
      entry.prevPrice = entry.price; entry.price = newPrice; entry.lastUpdate = now;
    } else if (!entry.prevPrice) { entry.prevPrice = entry.price; }
  }
  saveState();
}
function getItemPrice(id) { return (marketPrices && marketPrices[id]) ? marketPrices[id].price : (BASE_PRICES[id] || 100); }
function renderMarketTicker() {
  var el = document.getElementById('market-ticker-items'); if (!el || !marketPrices) return;
  var items = Object.keys(marketPrices).slice(0, 12); var html = '';
  items.forEach(function(id) {
    var entry = marketPrices[id]; var prev = entry.prevPrice || entry.price;
    var diff  = entry.price - prev;
    var pct   = prev > 0 ? ((diff / prev) * 100).toFixed(1) : '0.0';
    var cls   = diff >= 0 ? 'ticker-up' : 'ticker-down';
    var arrow = diff >= 0 ? '▲' : '▼';
    var name  = id.replace(/-/g, ' ').replace(/\b\w/g, function(c) { return c.toUpperCase(); });
    html += '<span class="ticker-item ' + cls + '">' + name + ' ⚡' + entry.price.toLocaleString() + ' ' + arrow + pct + '%</span>';
  });
  el.innerHTML = html + html;
}

// ── CASINO CORE ───────────────────────────────────────────────
var casinoGameActive = null;
var crashRunning = false, crashCashedOut = false, crashBet = 0, crashTarget = 1.0;

function openCasinoGame(game) {
  casinoGameActive = game;
  document.getElementById('casino-modal-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
  var titles = {slots:'🎰 Lucky Slots',dice:'🎲 Dice Roll',blackjack:'🃏 Blackjack',roulette:'🎡 Roulette',coinflip:'🪙 Coin Flip',crash:'📈 Crash',plinko:'🎯 Plinko',hilo:'🂡 Hi-Lo Cards',cscase:'📦 CS Cases',poker:'♠️ Video Poker',mines:'💣 Mines',baccarat:'🎴 Baccarat',crossy:'🐔 Crossy Road'};
  document.getElementById('casino-modal-title').textContent = titles[game] || game;
  var body = document.getElementById('casino-modal-body');
  if      (game === 'slots')     body.innerHTML = buildSlots();
  else if (game === 'dice')      body.innerHTML = buildDice();
  else if (game === 'blackjack') { body.innerHTML = buildBlackjack(); bjActive = false; }
  else if (game === 'roulette')  body.innerHTML = buildRoulette();
  else if (game === 'coinflip')  { body.innerHTML = buildCoinFlip(); coinChoice = null; }
  else if (game === 'crash')     body.innerHTML = buildCrash();
  else if (game === 'plinko')    { body.innerHTML = buildPlinko(); setTimeout(function() { initStakePlinko(); }, 80); }
  else if (game === 'hilo')      { body.innerHTML = buildHiLo(); initHiLo(); }
  else if (game === 'cscase')    { body.innerHTML = buildCSCases(); setTimeout(initCSCases, 50); }
  else if (game === 'poker')     { body.innerHTML = buildVideoPoker(); initVideoPoker(); }
  else if (game === 'mines')     { body.innerHTML = buildMines(); setTimeout(initMines, 50); }
  else if (game === 'baccarat')  { body.innerHTML = buildBaccarat(); baccaratSide = 'player'; }
  else if (game === 'crossy')    { body.innerHTML = buildCrossyRoad(); setTimeout(initCrossyRoad, 100); }
}
function closeCasinoGame() {
  document.getElementById('casino-modal-overlay').style.display = 'none';
  if (crashInterval) { clearInterval(crashInterval); crashInterval = null; }
  if (plinkoAnimId)  { cancelAnimationFrame(plinkoAnimId); plinkoAnimId = null; }
  if (cxRAFId)       { cancelAnimationFrame(cxRAFId);      cxRAFId = null; }
  crashRunning = false; casinoGameActive = null;
}
function closeCasinoModal(e) { if (e.target === document.getElementById('casino-modal-overlay')) closeCasinoGame(); }
function addLiveBet(user, game, amount, profit) {
  if (user === 'You' && amount > 0) {
    var returned = amount + profit;
    var mult = returned > 0 ? (returned / amount) : 0;
    updateCasinoLastResult(game, amount, returned, mult);
    if (profit > 0 && typeof addXP !== 'undefined') addXP(Math.max(1, Math.floor(profit / 10)));
    if (typeof trackDC !== 'undefined') {
      trackDC('total_bet', amount);
      if (profit > 0) {
        trackDC('casino_wins', 1);
        if (game === 'Lucky Slots') trackDC('slots_win', 1);
        if (game === 'Blackjack')   trackDC('bj_win', 1);
        if (game === 'Plinko')      trackDC('plinko_play', 1);
        if (mult >= 10)             trackDC('crash10', 1);
        if (_csSession && _csSession.profit > 0) trackDC('net_positive', 1);
      }
      if (game === 'Plinko') trackDC('plinko_play', 1);
    }
  }
  var c = document.getElementById('live-bets-container'); if (!c) return;
  var isWin = profit > 0;
  var colors = ['#7c3aed','#059669','#d97706','#dc2626','#0891b2','#9333ea','#b45309'];
  var color = colors[user.charCodeAt(0) % colors.length];
  var mult = amount > 0 ? ((Math.abs(profit) + amount) / amount).toFixed(2) : '—';
  var div = document.createElement('div'); div.className = 'lb-row';
  div.innerHTML = '<div class="lb-avatar" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,'+color+','+color+'99)">'+user.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+'</div>'
    +'<span class="lb-user">'+user+'***</span><span class="lb-game">'+game+'</span>'
    +'<span class="lb-amt">⚡'+Math.abs(amount).toFixed(0)+'</span>'
    +(isWin?'<span style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.3);font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;min-width:38px;text-align:right;flex-shrink:0">'+mult+'×</span>':'<span style="min-width:38px;flex-shrink:0"></span>')
    +'<span class="lb-res '+(isWin?'lb-win':'lb-lose')+'">'+(isWin?'+':'-')+'⚡'+Math.abs(profit).toFixed(0)+'</span>';
  c.insertBefore(div, c.firstChild);
  if (c.children.length > 10) c.removeChild(c.lastChild);
  var cnt = document.getElementById('live-bets-count');
  if (cnt) cnt.textContent = c.children.length + ' bets';
}
function casinoFilter(btn, cat) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.casino-filter-btn').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('active'); });
  btn.classList.add('active');
  document.querySelectorAll('#view-casino .casino-game-card').forEach(function(card) {
    card.style.display = (cat === 'all' || card.dataset.cat === cat) ? '' : 'none';
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('#view-casino .casino-section-title').forEach(function(s) {
    if (cat === 'all') { s.style.display = ''; return; }
    var grid = s.nextElementSibling; if (!grid) return;
    var visible = Array.from(grid.querySelectorAll('.casino-game-card')).some(function(c){ return c.style.display !== 'none'; });
    s.style.display = visible ? '' : 'none'; grid.style.display = visible ? '' : 'none';
  });
}
function getBet(id)    { var v=parseFloat(document.getElementById(id)?document.getElementById(id).value:0); return isNaN(v)||v<=0?0:v; }
function halfBet(id)   { var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el)el.value=Math.max(1,Math.floor(parseFloat(el.value||10)/2)); }
function doubleBet(id) { var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el)el.value=Math.min(stormCoins,Math.floor(parseFloat(el.value||10)*2)); }
function maxBet(id)    { var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el)el.value=stormCoins; }

function slotsUpdateTotal(){var b=parseFloat(document.getElementById('slots-bet').value)||10;var t=document.getElementById('slots-total');if(t)t.textContent=(b*slotsLines).toFixed(0);}
function slotsSetLines(n){slotsLines=n;['1','3','5'].forEach(function(x){var b=document.getElementById('lines-'+x);if(b){b.style.background=parseInt(x)===n?'rgba(124,58,237,0.3)':'';b.style.borderColor=parseInt(x)===n?'var(--accent)':'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)';}});slotsUpdateTotal();}
function spinSlots(){
  var bpl=getBet('slots-bet');if(!bpl){showToast('Enter bet');return;}
  var total=bpl*slotsLines;if(total>stormCoins){showToast('Not enough coins!');return;}
  updateCoins(-total);
  var btn=document.getElementById('slots-btn');btn.disabled=true;btn.textContent='🎰 Spinning...';
  var cols=[0,1,2,3,4].map(function(i){return document.getElementById('rc'+i);});
  cols.forEach(function(c){if(c)c.classList.add('spinning');});
  var ticks=0,iv=setInterval(function(){
    [0,1,2,3,4].forEach(function(i){var r=document.getElementById('r'+i);if(r){var s=SYMS[Math.floor(Math.random()*SYMS.length)];r.textContent=s;r.style.color=SYM_CLR[s]||'#fff';}});
    ticks++;if(ticks>22){
      clearInterval(iv);
      var rand=Math.random(),final;
      if(rand<0.3){var sym=SYMS[Math.floor(Math.random()*SYMS.length)];var cnt=[3,3,4,5][Math.floor(Math.random()*4)];final=Array(5).fill('').map(function(_,i){return i<cnt?sym:SYMS[Math.floor(Math.random()*SYMS.length)];});}
      else{final=Array(5).fill('').map(function(){return SYMS[Math.floor(Math.random()*SYMS.length)];});}
      cols.forEach(function(c,i){if(c)setTimeout(function(){c.classList.remove('spinning');},i*80);});
      setTimeout(function(){[0,1,2,3,4].forEach(function(i){var r=document.getElementById('r'+i);if(r){r.textContent=final[i];r.style.color=SYM_CLR[final[i]]||'#fff';}});evalSlots(final,bpl,total,btn);},420);
    }
  },68);
}
function evalSlots(reels,bpl,total,btn){
  var counts={};reels.forEach(function(s){counts[s]=(counts[s]||0)+1;});
  var maxC=Math.max.apply(null,Object.values(counts));
  var sym=Object.keys(counts).find(function(k){return counts[k]===maxC;});
  var mult=0;if(SYM_PAY[sym]&&SYM_PAY[sym][String(maxC)])mult=SYM_PAY[sym][String(maxC)];
  var res=document.getElementById('slots-result');
  if(mult>0){var prize=bpl*mult*slotsLines;updateCoins(prize);var isJack=sym==='7️⃣'&&maxC===5;if(isJack&&typeof trackAch!=='undefined')trackAch('slots777',1);res.innerHTML='<div class="result-win-txt">'+(isJack?'🎉 JACKPOT!! ':'🎉 WIN! ')+'⚡+'+(prize).toFixed(0)+' ('+mult+'×)</div>';showToast((isJack?'🎰 JACKPOT!! ':'🎰 WIN! ')+'⚡+'+(prize-total).toFixed(0));addLiveBet('You','Slots',total,prize-total);spawnParticles(isJack?['🎰','7️⃣','⭐','💰','🎉']:['🎰','⭐','💰'],isJack?20:8);}
  else{res.innerHTML='<div class="result-lose-txt">💸 No match — try again!</div>';addLiveBet('You','Slots',total,-total);}
  btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent='🎰 SPIN';if(typeof trackAch!=='undefined')trackAch('bets',1);
}

function buildDice(){
