<!-- ============================================================
  NOVYX — PART 10: CROSSY ROAD CASINO
  ============================================================ -->
<script>
var cxBet=0,cxRow=0,cxActive=false,cxDead=false;
var cxRAFId=null,cxLanes=[],cxCars=[],cxCamY=0;
var cxPlayer={x:0,y:0},cxTargetY=0,cxMoving=false;
var CX_MULTS=[1.0,1.5,2.2,3.1,4.4,6.3,9.0,13.0,19.0,28.0,42.0,65.0,100.0];
var CX_TS=48;

function buildCrossyRoad(){
  return '<div style="display:flex;min-height:480px">'
    +'<div style="width:180px;flex-shrink:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.25);border-right:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06);padding:20px 16px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:12px">'
    +'<div><div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted);font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;margin-bottom:6px">Bet</div>'
    +'<input class="bet-inp" id="cx-bet" type="number" value="10" min="1" style="width:100%;margin-bottom:6px">'
    +'<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:4px"><button class="bet-btn" onclick="halfBet(\'cx-bet\')">½</button><button class="bet-btn" onclick="doubleBet(\'cx-bet\')">2×</button><button class="bet-btn" onclick="maxBet(\'cx-bet\')">Max</button></div></div>'
    +'<button class="play-btn" id="cx-start" onclick="startCrossy()">Start</button>'
    +'<button class="play-btn" id="cx-hop" disabled onclick="cxHop()" style="font-size:18px">🐔 Hop!</button>'
    +'<button class="play-btn" id="cx-cashout" disabled onclick="cxCashout()" style="background:rgba(16,185,129,0.12);border:1px solid rgba(16,185,129,0.3);color:#10b981">Cash Out</button>'
    +'<div id="cx-mult" style="text-align:center;font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:#f59e0b;min-height:32px">1.00×</div>'
    +'<div id="cx-row-disp" style="text-align:center;font-size:12px;color:var(--muted)">Row 0</div>'
    +'<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted);line-height:1.6">Hop across lanes to multiply your bet.<br>Hit a car = BUST.<br><br>Arrow Up or W to hop.</div>'
    +'</div>'
    +'<div style="flex:1;position:relative;overflow:hidden">'
    +'<canvas id="cx-canvas" style="display:block;width:100%;height:100%;min-height:400px"></canvas>'
    +'</div></div>';
}

function startCrossy(){
  var bet=getBet('cx-bet');if(!bet)return;
  if(bet>stormCoins){showToast('Not enough coins!');return;}
  updateCoins(-bet);cxBet=bet;cxRow=0;cxActive=true;cxDead=false;cxMoving=false;cxCamY=0;
  var cv=document.getElementById('cx-canvas');if(!cv)return;
  var rect=cv.getBoundingClientRect();
  cv.width=rect.width||440;cv.height=rect.height||400;
  var W=cv.width,H=cv.height,ts=CX_TS;
  var cols=Math.floor(W/ts);
  cxPlayer={x:Math.floor(cols/2)*ts+ts/2,y:H-ts-4};cxTargetY=cxPlayer.y;
  cxLanes=[];cxCars=[];
  for(var r=0;r<30;r++){
    var spd=(0.5+Math.random()*1.8)*(Math.random()<0.5?1:-1);
    cxLanes.push({y:H-ts*(r+2),speed:spd,dark:r%2===0});
    var n=Math.floor(1+Math.random()*3);
    for(var c=0;c<n;c++){cxCars.push({lane:r,x:Math.random()*W*2,w:38+Math.floor(Math.random()*22),h:24,speed:spd});}
  }
  document.getElementById('cx-start').disabled=true;
  document.getElementById('cx-hop').disabled=false;
  document.getElementById('cx-cashout').disabled=true;
  document.getElementById('cx-mult').textContent='1.00×';
  document.getElementById('cx-row-disp').textContent='Row 0';
  if(cxRAFId)cancelAnimationFrame(cxRAFId);
  cxLoop();
}

function cxLoop(){
  var cv=document.getElementById('cx-canvas');if(!cv||!cxActive)return;
  var ctx=cv.getContext('2d'),W=cv.width,H=cv.height,ts=CX_TS;
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);ctx.fillStyle='#060e1a';ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  if(cxMoving){
    cxPlayer.y+=(cxTargetY-cxPlayer.y)*0.2;
    if(Math.abs(cxPlayer.y-cxTargetY)<0.8){cxPlayer.y=cxTargetY;cxMoving=false;}
  }
  cxLanes.forEach(function(lane){
    var dy=lane.y+cxCamY;if(dy<-ts||dy>H+ts)return;
    ctx.fillStyle=lane.dark?'#0e1a0e':'#111f11';ctx.fillRect(0,dy,W,ts);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.06)';ctx.fillRect(0,dy+ts-1,W,1);
  });
  ctx.fillStyle='#071207';ctx.fillRect(0,H-ts,W,ts);
  cxCars.forEach(function(car){
    car.x+=car.speed;
    if(car.speed>0&&car.x>W+car.w)car.x=-car.w;
    if(car.speed<0&&car.x<-car.w)car.x=W+car.w;
    var lane=cxLanes[car.lane];if(!lane)return;
    var cy=lane.y+cxCamY+(ts-car.h)/2;
    if(cy<-car.h||cy>H+car.h)return;
    ctx.fillStyle=car.speed>0?'#dc2626':'#2563eb';
    ctx.beginPath();
    if(ctx.roundRect)ctx.roundRect(car.x,cy,car.w,car.h,4);
    else ctx.rect(car.x,cy,car.w,car.h);
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.fillStyle='#fef08a';
    var lx=car.speed>0?car.x+car.w-5:car.x+2;
    ctx.fillRect(lx,cy+3,3,5);ctx.fillRect(lx,cy+car.h-8,3,5);
  });
  if(!cxDead&&!cxMoving){
    var px=cxPlayer.x-12,py=cxPlayer.y+cxCamY+8,pw=24,ph=20;
    cxCars.forEach(function(car){
      if(cxDead)return;
      var lane=cxLanes[car.lane];if(!lane)return;
      var cy=lane.y+cxCamY+(ts-car.h)/2;
      if(px<car.x+car.w&&px+pw>car.x&&py<cy+car.h&&py+ph>cy){
        cxDead=true;cxActive=false;
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(220,38,38,0.55)';ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        ctx.fillStyle='#fff';ctx.font='bold 36px Rajdhani,sans-serif';ctx.textAlign='center';
        ctx.fillText('💥 SPLAT!',W/2,H/2);
        showToast('💥 Got hit! Lost ⚡'+cxBet);
        addLiveBet('You','Crossy Road',cxBet,-cxBet);
        document.getElementById('cx-start').disabled=false;
        document.getElementById('cx-hop').disabled=true;
        document.getElementById('cx-cashout').disabled=true;
      }
    });
  }
  ctx.font=ts*0.7+'px serif';ctx.textAlign='left';
  ctx.fillText('🐔',cxPlayer.x-ts*0.35,cxPlayer.y+ts*0.65+cxCamY);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.9)';ctx.font='bold 13px Rajdhani,sans-serif';ctx.textAlign='left';
  ctx.fillText('Row '+cxRow+'  ×'+CX_MULTS[Math.min(cxRow,CX_MULTS.length-1)].toFixed(2),8,20);
  if(cxActive)cxRAFId=requestAnimationFrame(cxLoop);
}

function cxHop(){
  if(!cxActive||cxMoving||cxDead)return;
  cxRow++;
  cxCamY+=CX_TS;cxMoving=true;
  var m=CX_MULTS[Math.min(cxRow,CX_MULTS.length-1)];
  document.getElementById('cx-mult').textContent=m.toFixed(2)+'×';
  document.getElementById('cx-row-disp').textContent='Row '+cxRow;
  document.getElementById('cx-cashout').disabled=false;
  if(cxRow>=12)cxCashout();
}

function cxCashout(){
  if(!cxActive||cxRow===0){if(cxRow===0)showToast('Hop at least once first!');return;}
  cxActive=false;
  var m=CX_MULTS[Math.min(cxRow,CX_MULTS.length-1)];
  var prize=Math.round(cxBet*m);
  updateCoins(prize);
  showToast('🐔 Row '+cxRow+' — '+m.toFixed(2)+'×! ⚡+'+(prize-cxBet));
  addLiveBet('You','Crossy Road',cxBet,prize-cxBet);spawnParticles(['🐔','⚡','💰'],8);
  document.getElementById('cx-start').disabled=false;
  document.getElementById('cx-hop').disabled=true;
  document.getElementById('cx-cashout').disabled=true;
}

document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
  if(e.key==='ArrowUp'||e.key==='w'||e.key==='W')cxHop();
});
</script>

  { id:'ach-bet25',    group:'casino',    tier:'silver', icon:'🎰', name:'Regular Gambler',    desc:'Place 25 casino bets.',              goal:25,  stat:'bets',     reward:400  },

var achStats={}, achClaimed={};

function loadAchData(){
  achStats   = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_ach_stats')   || '{}');
  achClaimed = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gv_ach_claimed') || '{}');
}
function saveAchData(){
  localStorage.setItem('gv_ach_stats',   JSON.stringify(achStats));
  localStorage.setItem('gv_ach_claimed', JSON.stringify(achClaimed));
}

function trackAch(stat, value){
  loadAchData();
  if(value===undefined)value=1;
  achStats[stat]=(achStats[stat]||0)+value;
  saveAchData();
  checkAchievements();
}

function getAchStat(stat){
  if(stat==='played')  return recent.length;
  if(stat==='library') return library.length;
  if(stat==='horror')  return recent.filter(function(g){return g.genre==='Horror';}).length;
  if(stat==='achCount'){
    return ACHIEVEMENTS.filter(function(a){return a.stat!=='achCount'&&achClaimed[a.id];}).length;
  }
  return achStats[stat]||0;
}

function checkAchievements(){
  ACHIEVEMENTS.forEach(function(ach){
    if(achClaimed[ach.id])return;
    var val=getAchStat(ach.stat);
    if(val>=ach.goal&&!achStats['_notified_'+ach.id]){
      achStats['_notified_'+ach.id]=1;
      saveAchData();
      showToast('🏆 Achievement unlocked: '+ach.name+'! Claim ⚡'+ach.reward);
    }
  });
}

function claimAch(id){
  var ach=ACHIEVEMENTS.find(function(a){return a.id===id;});
  if(!ach||achClaimed[id])return;
  var val=getAchStat(ach.stat);
  if(val<ach.goal){showToast('Not completed yet!');return;}
  achClaimed[id]=Date.now();
  saveAchData();
  updateCoins(ach.reward);
  spawnParticles(['🏆','⚡','✨'],10);
  showToast('🏆 Claimed '+ach.name+'! +⚡'+ach.reward.toLocaleString());
  renderAchievements();
}

function renderAchievements(){
  loadAchData();
  var totalComplete=0,totalCoinsEarned=0;
  ['explorer','casino','collector','legend'].forEach(function(group){
    var grid=document.getElementById('ach-grid-'+group);if(!grid)return;
    grid.innerHTML='';
    var groupAchs=ACHIEVEMENTS.filter(function(a){return a.group===group;});
    groupAchs.forEach(function(ach){
      var val=getAchStat(ach.stat);
      var pct=Math.min(100,Math.round((val/ach.goal)*100));
      var done=val>=ach.goal;
      var claimed=!!achClaimed[ach.id];
      var canClaim=done&&!claimed;
      if(claimed){totalComplete++;totalCoinsEarned+=ach.reward;}
      var card=document.createElement('div');
      card.className='ach-card'+(claimed?' ach-done':done?'':(pct===0?' ach-locked':''));
      var progressBar='<div class="ach-progress-bar"><div class="ach-progress-fill tier-'+ach.tier+'" style="width:'+pct+'%"></div></div>'
        +'<div class="ach-progress-txt"><span>'+val.toLocaleString()+' / '+ach.goal.toLocaleString()+'</span><span class="ach-reward">⚡'+ach.reward.toLocaleString()+'</span></div>';
      var actionHtml=claimed
        ?'<div class="ach-claimed-badge">✓ Claimed ⚡'+ach.reward.toLocaleString()+'</div>'
        :canClaim
        ?'<button class="ach-claim-btn" onclick="claimAch(\''+ach.id+'\')">Claim ⚡'+ach.reward.toLocaleString()+'</button>'
        :'';
      card.innerHTML='<div class="ach-icon-wrap tier-'+ach.tier+'">'+(claimed?ach.icon:(pct===0?'🔒':ach.icon))+'</div>'
        +'<div class="ach-body">'
        +'<div class="ach-name">'+ach.name+'</div>'
        +'<div class="ach-desc">'+ach.desc+'</div>'
        +progressBar+actionHtml
        +'</div>';
      grid.appendChild(card);
    });
  });
  var el=document.getElementById('ach-count');
  var ec=document.getElementById('ach-coins-earned');
  var et=document.getElementById('ach-total');
  if(el)el.textContent=totalComplete;
  if(ec)ec.textContent=totalCoinsEarned.toLocaleString();
  if(et)et.textContent=ACHIEVEMENTS.length;
}

function shopSetFilter(btn,cat){
  document.querySelectorAll('.shop-filter-btn').forEach(function(b){b.classList.remove('active');});
  btn.classList.add('active');
  renderCoinShop(cat);
}

function renderCoinShop(filterCat){
  var grid=document.getElementById('coin-shop-grid');if(!grid)return;
  var cat=filterCat||'all';
  if(!filterCat){
    var activeBtn=document.querySelector('.shop-filter-btn.active');
    cat=activeBtn?(activeBtn.dataset.cat||'all'):'all';
  }
  var items=cat==='all'?SHOP_CATALOGUE:SHOP_CATALOGUE.filter(function(i){return i.cat===cat;});
  grid.innerHTML=items.map(function(item){
    var owned=item.free||ownedItems.indexOf(item.id)!==-1;
    var equipped=equippedItems[item.cat]===item.id;
    var canAfford=stormCoins>=item.price;
    var cantAfford=!owned&&!canAfford;
    var badgeHtml=equipped?'<div class="shop-item-badge equipped">EQUIPPED</div>'
      :owned?'<div class="shop-item-badge owned">OWNED</div>':'';
    var btnHtml=equipped
      ?'<button class="shop-item-btn unequip" onclick="shopUnequip(\''+item.id+'\',\''+item.cat+'\')">Unequip</button>'
      :owned
      ?'<button class="shop-item-btn equip" onclick="shopEquip(\''+item.id+'\',\''+item.cat+'\')">✓ Equip</button>'
      :cantAfford
      ?'<button class="shop-item-btn disabled" disabled>⚡ '+item.price.toLocaleString()+'</button>'
      :'<button class="shop-item-btn buy" onclick="shopBuy(\''+item.id+'\')">Buy · ⚡'+item.price.toLocaleString()+'</button>';
    return '<div class="shop-item-card'+(equipped?' equipped':owned?' owned':'')+(cantAfford?' cant-afford':'')+'" data-cat="'+item.cat+'">'
      +'<div class="shop-item-emoji">'+item.emoji+'</div>'
      +badgeHtml
      +'<div class="shop-item-name">'+item.name+'</div>'
      +'<div class="shop-item-desc">'+item.desc+'</div>'
      +btnHtml+'</div>';
  }).join('');
  var balEl=document.getElementById('shop-balance-display');
  if(balEl)balEl.textContent=stormCoins.toLocaleString();
}

function shopBuy(id){
  var item=SHOP_CATALOGUE.find(function(i){return i.id===id;});
  if(!item||stormCoins<item.price){showToast('Not enough coins!');return;}
  updateCoins(-item.price);
  if(ownedItems.indexOf(id)===-1)ownedItems.push(id);
  saveState();
  spawnParticles(['✨','⚡'],6);
  showToast('✓ Purchased: '+item.name+'!');
  renderCoinShop();
}

function shopEquip(id,cat){
  var item=SHOP_CATALOGUE.find(function(i){return i.id===id;});
  if(!item)return;
  if(!item.free&&ownedItems.indexOf(id)===-1){showToast("You don't own this!");return;}
  equippedItems[cat]=id;
  saveState();applyEquippedFrame();
  showToast('Equipped: '+item.name);
  renderCoinShop();
}

function shopUnequip(id,cat){
  var item=SHOP_CATALOGUE.find(function(i){return i.id===id;});
  delete equippedItems[cat];
  saveState();applyEquippedFrame();
  showToast('Unequipped'+(item?': '+item.name:''));
  renderCoinShop();
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NAV RING — CANVAS RENDERER (draws pill border light precisely)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var _navRingAngle = 0;
var _navRingRAF = null;
var _navRingPill = null;


// ── PREMIUM MOVING STARFIELD ─────────────────────────────────
(function initStarfield(){
  var cv=document.getElementById('starfield-canvas');
  if(!cv)return;
  var ctx=cv.getContext('2d');
  var stars=[], shooters=[], W, H;

  function resize(){ W=cv.width=window.innerWidth; H=cv.height=window.innerHeight; }
  resize(); window.addEventListener('resize',resize);

  // Create 3 depth layers of stars
  for(var i=0;i<260;i++){
    var depth=Math.random(); // 0=far,1=near
    stars.push({
      x:Math.random()*W, y:Math.random()*H,
      r: 0.25 + depth*1.8,
      vy: 0.04 + depth*0.18,  // vertical drift speed
      vx: (Math.random()-0.5)*0.04,
      tw: Math.random()*Math.PI*2,
      twSpd: 0.006+Math.random()*0.018,
      baseAlpha: 0.25 + depth*0.65,
      col: Math.random()<0.07?'#c4b5fd':Math.random()<0.05?'#93c5fd':'#ffffff'
    });
  }

  function spawnShooter(){
    shooters.push({
      x: Math.random()*W*0.6+W*0.05,
      y: Math.random()*H*0.45,
      len: 90+Math.random()*140,
      spd: 7+Math.random()*10,
      ang: Math.PI/4+(Math.random()-0.5)*0.35,
      life: 1.0,
      decay: 0.018+Math.random()*0.022
    });
  }
  setInterval(function(){ if(Math.random()<0.4) spawnShooter(); }, 3000);

  function tick(){
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);

    // Stars
    for(var i=0;i<stars.length;i++){
      var s=stars[i];
      s.tw+=s.twSpd;
      s.y+=s.vy; s.x+=s.vx;
      if(s.y>H+2){ s.y=-2; s.x=Math.random()*W; }
      if(s.x<-2)s.x=W+2; if(s.x>W+2)s.x=-2;
      var a=s.baseAlpha*(0.55+0.45*Math.sin(s.tw));
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(s.x,s.y,s.r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle=s.col; ctx.globalAlpha=a; ctx.fill();
      if(s.r>1.3){
        ctx.globalAlpha=a*0.3;
        ctx.strokeStyle=s.col; ctx.lineWidth=0.5;
        var cl=s.r*3.5;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(s.x-cl,s.y); ctx.lineTo(s.x+cl,s.y);
        ctx.moveTo(s.x,s.y-cl); ctx.lineTo(s.x,s.y+cl);
        ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
    ctx.globalAlpha=1;

    // Shooting stars
    for(var j=shooters.length-1;j>=0;j--){
      var sh=shooters[j];
      var tx=Math.cos(sh.ang)*sh.len, ty=Math.sin(sh.ang)*sh.len;
      var g=ctx.createLinearGradient(sh.x,sh.y,sh.x+tx,sh.y+ty);
      g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,255,255,'+sh.life+')');
      g.addColorStop(0.25,'rgba(210,180,255,'+(sh.life*0.6)+')');
      g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(sh.x,sh.y); ctx.lineTo(sh.x+tx,sh.y+ty);
      ctx.strokeStyle=g; ctx.lineWidth=1.8; ctx.globalAlpha=sh.life; ctx.stroke();
      ctx.globalAlpha=1;
      sh.x+=Math.cos(sh.ang)*sh.spd;
      sh.y+=Math.sin(sh.ang)*sh.spd;
      sh.life-=sh.decay;
      if(sh.life<=0) shooters.splice(j,1);
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(tick);
  }
  tick();
})();

function initNavRingCanvas() {
  var canvas = document.getElementById('nav-ring-canvas');
  if (!canvas) return;
  var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  function resize() { canvas.width = window.innerWidth; canvas.height = 80; }
  resize(); window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  function getColor() {
    var s = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement);
    return { a:(s.getPropertyValue('--nav-ring-a').trim()||'#7c3aed'), a2:(s.getPropertyValue('--nav-ring-a2').trim()||'#a855f7') };
  }
  function hexToRgb(hex) {
    hex = hex.replace('#','');
    if (hex.length===3) hex=hex.split('').map(function(c){return c+c;}).join('');
    var n=parseInt(hex,16); return [(n>>16)&255,(n>>8)&255,n&255];
  }
  function draw() {
    var pill = document.querySelector('.topnav');
    if (!pill) { _navRingRAF=requestAnimationFrame(draw); return; }
    var r = pill.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (!r||r.width===0) { _navRingRAF=requestAnimationFrame(draw); return; }
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height);
    var x=r.left,y=r.top,w=r.width,h=r.height,rad=h/2,pad=1.5;
    x-=pad; y-=pad; w+=pad*2; h+=pad*2; rad+=pad;
    var col=getColor(), ca=hexToRgb(col.a), ca2=hexToRgb(col.a2);
    var sw=w-2*rad, sh=h-2*rad, perim=2*sw+2*sh+2*Math.PI*rad;
    var spotLen=perim*0.18, dist=(_navRingAngle/360)*perim;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x+rad,y); ctx.lineTo(x+w-rad,y);
    ctx.arcTo(x+w,y,x+w,y+rad,rad); ctx.lineTo(x+w,y+h-rad);
    ctx.arcTo(x+w,y+h,x+w-rad,y+h,rad); ctx.lineTo(x+rad,y+h);
    ctx.arcTo(x,y+h,x,y+h-rad,rad); ctx.lineTo(x,y+rad);
    ctx.arcTo(x,y,x+rad,y,rad); ctx.closePath();
    ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.06)'; ctx.lineWidth=1; ctx.stroke();
    function pp(d) {
      d=((d%perim)+perim)%perim;
      var al=Math.PI/2*rad;
      if(d<sw) return {px:x+rad+d,py:y}; d-=sw;
      if(d<al){var a=-Math.PI/2+(d/rad);return{px:x+w-rad+Math.cos(a)*rad,py:y+rad+Math.sin(a)*rad};} d-=al;
      if(d<sh) return {px:x+w,py:y+rad+d}; d-=sh;
      if(d<al){var a2=d/rad;return{px:x+w-rad+Math.cos(a2)*rad,py:y+h-rad+Math.sin(a2)*rad};} d-=al;
      if(d<sw) return {px:x+w-rad-d,py:y+h}; d-=sw;
      if(d<al){var a3=Math.PI/2+(d/rad);return{px:x+rad+Math.cos(a3)*rad,py:y+h-rad+Math.sin(a3)*rad};} d-=al;
      if(d<sh) return {px:x,py:y+h-rad-d}; d-=sh;
      var a4=Math.PI+(d/rad);return{px:x+rad+Math.cos(a4)*rad,py:y+rad+Math.sin(a4)*rad};
    }
    var steps=60;
    for(var i=0;i<=steps;i++){
      var t=i/steps, dp=dist+(t-1)*spotLen, pt=pp(dp);
      var alpha=t<0.3?t/0.3:t>0.85?(1-t)/0.15:1; alpha=Math.max(0,Math.min(1,alpha));
      var r2=Math.round(ca[0]+(ca2[0]-ca[0])*t),g2=Math.round(ca[1]+(ca2[1]-ca[1])*t),b2=Math.round(ca[2]+(ca2[2]-ca[2])*t);
      if(i<steps){var pt2=pp(dp+spotLen/steps);ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pt.px,pt.py);ctx.lineTo(pt2.px,pt2.py);ctx.strokeStyle='rgba('+r2+','+g2+','+b2+','+alpha+')';ctx.lineWidth=t>0.8?3:2;ctx.lineCap='round';ctx.stroke();}
      if(t>0.85){ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(pt.px,pt.py,2.5*(t-0.85)/0.15,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,'+(alpha*0.9)+')';ctx.fill();}
    }
    var head=pp(dist),grd=ctx.createRadialGradient(head.px,head.py,0,head.px,head.py,20);
    grd.addColorStop(0,'rgba('+ca2[0]+','+ca2[1]+','+ca2[2]+',0.6)');
    grd.addColorStop(1,'rgba('+ca2[0]+','+ca2[1]+','+ca2[2]+',0)');
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(head.px,head.py,20,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=grd;ctx.fill();
    _navRingAngle=(_navRingAngle+0.6)%360;
    _navRingRAF=requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  }
  draw();
}

// ── STREAK ENERGY SYSTEM ─────────────────────────────────────
/*
  Streak = days in a row visiting/playing.
  Tracked by storing last-visit date in localStorage.
  Tiers: 1=Warm(gold) 3=Hot(orange) 5=Fire(red) 7=Legend(purple) 10=Cosmic(cyan)
  XP multiplier: streak * 0.1 + 1.0  (10% bonus per day, up to 3x at 20 days)
  Badges & username glow applied to account button.
*/
var _streak = 0;
var _streakXP = 1.0;

var STREAK_TIERS = [
  { days:1,  label:'Warm',   emoji:'🔥',  cls:'s1', glow:false  },
  { days:3,  label:'Hot',    emoji:'🔥🔥', cls:'s2', glow:false  },
  { days:5,  label:'Fire',   emoji:'🔥🔥🔥',cls:'s3', glow:'streak-glow-3' },
  { days:7,  label:'Legend', emoji:'👑',  cls:'s4', glow:'streak-glow-3' },
  { days:10, label:'Cosmic', emoji:'✨',  cls:'s5', glow:'streak-glow-5' },
];

function getStreakTier(days) {
  var tier = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < STREAK_TIERS.length; i++) {
    if (days >= STREAK_TIERS[i].days) tier = STREAK_TIERS[i];
  }
  return tier;
}

function loadStreak() {
  var today     = new Date().toDateString();
  var lastVisit = localStorage.getItem('gv_streak_last') || '';
  var count     = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('gv_streak_count') || '0');

  if (lastVisit === today) {
    // Already visited today — just restore
    _streak = count;
  } else {
    var yesterday = new Date();
    yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1);
    if (lastVisit === yesterday.toDateString()) {
      // Consecutive day — increment
      count++;
      _streak = count;
      localStorage.setItem('gv_streak_count', count);
      localStorage.setItem('gv_streak_last', today);
      // Toast if milestone
      var tier = getStreakTier(count);
      if (tier && [1,3,5,7,10,14,21,30].indexOf(count) !== -1) {
        setTimeout(function() {
          showToast(tier.emoji + ' ' + count + '-Day Streak! ' + tier.label + ' · ' + streakXPLabel(count), { icon: tier.emoji });
        }, 1200);
      }
    } else if (lastVisit === '') {
      // First ever visit
      _streak = 1;
      localStorage.setItem('gv_streak_count', 1);
      localStorage.setItem('gv_streak_last', today);
    } else {
      // Streak broken
      var old = count;
      _streak = 1;
      localStorage.setItem('gv_streak_count', 1);
      localStorage.setItem('gv_streak_last', today);
      if (old >= 3) {
        setTimeout(function() {
          showToast('💔 Streak lost after ' + old + ' days. Starting fresh!');
        }, 1200);
      }
    }
  }

  _streakXP = Math.min(3.0, 1.0 + _streak * 0.1);
  updateStreakUI();
  if (typeof updateRankStreakPill !== 'undefined') updateRankStreakPill();
}

function streakXPLabel(days) {
  var mult = Math.min(3.0, 1.0 + days * 0.1);
  return mult.toFixed(1) + '× XP';
}

function updateStreakUI() {
  if (_streak < 1) return;
  var tier = getStreakTier(_streak);

  // Nav streak bar
  var wrap  = document.getElementById('streak-bar-wrap');
  var fill  = document.getElementById('streak-bar-fill');
  var label = document.getElementById('streak-bar-label');
  var emoji = document.getElementById('streak-bar-emoji');

  if (wrap) wrap.style.display = 'flex';

  if (tier) {
    var colors = { s1:'#f59e0b', s2:'#f97316', s3:'#ef4444', s4:'#a855f7', s5:'#06b6d4' };
    var col = colors[tier.cls] || '#f59e0b';
    if (fill) {
      // Fill % = progress to next tier milestone
      var tiers = STREAK_TIERS.map(function(t){ return t.days; });
      var idx   = STREAK_TIERS.indexOf(tier);
      var next  = idx < STREAK_TIERS.length-1 ? STREAK_TIERS[idx+1].days : tier.days + 10;
      var prev  = tier.days;
      var pct   = Math.min(100, Math.round((_streak - prev) / (next - prev) * 100));
      fill.style.width = pct + '%';
      fill.style.background = 'linear-gradient(90deg,' + col + ',' + col + 'cc)';
    }
    if (label) { label.textContent = _streak + 'd'; label.style.color = col; }
    if (emoji) emoji.textContent = tier.emoji.split('')[0];
  } else {
    if (fill) fill.style.width = (_streak * 33) + '%';
    if (label) { label.textContent = _streak + 'd'; }
  }

  // Account button — apply glow to username label
  var lbl = document.getElementById('account-label');
  if (lbl && tier && tier.glow) {
    lbl.className = tier.glow;
  }

  // Update streak badge in account modal
  var badge = document.getElementById('streak-modal-badge');
  if (badge && tier) {
    badge.innerHTML = '<span class="streak-badge ' + tier.cls + '">' + tier.emoji + ' ' + _streak + '-Day Streak · ' + tier.label + '</span>';
  }
}

function showStreakInfo() {
  var tier = getStreakTier(_streak);
  var msg  = _streak + '-day streak';
  if (tier) msg += ' · ' + tier.label + ' · ' + streakXPLabel(_streak) + ' multiplier';
  showToast('🔥 ' + msg, { icon: '🔥' });
}

// ── FX WALLPAPER SYSTEM ──────────────────────────────────────
var _fxCanvas   = null;
var _fxCtx      = null;
var _fxRAF      = null;
var _fxCurrent  = null;

function fxInit() {
  _fxCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  _fxCanvas.id = 'fx-wallpaper';
  _fxCanvas.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:1;pointer-events:none;opacity:0;transition:opacity 0.8s ease;';
  document.body.insertBefore(_fxCanvas, document.body.firstChild);
  _fxCtx = _fxCanvas.getContext('2d');
  function resize() { _fxCanvas.width=window.innerWidth; _fxCanvas.height=window.innerHeight; }
  resize(); window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
}

function fxActivate(btn, id) {
  fxStop();
  _fxCurrent = id;
  document.querySelectorAll('.fxb-btn').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('active'); });
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  _fxCanvas.style.opacity = '1';
  _fxCtx.clearRect(0,0,_fxCanvas.width,_fxCanvas.height);
  var tickFn = FX_EFFECTS[id];
  if (!tickFn) return;
  var state = tickFn(_fxCanvas, _fxCtx);
  function loop() {
    if (_fxCurrent !== id) return;
    state();
    _fxRAF = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  loop();
}

function fxToggleBar() {
  var wrap = document.getElementById('fx-bar-wrap');
  var showBtn = document.getElementById('fx-show-btn');
  if (!wrap) return;
  var hiding = !wrap.classList.contains('hidden');
  wrap.classList.toggle('hidden', hiding);
  if (showBtn) showBtn.style.display = hiding ? 'block' : 'none';
}

function fxStop() {
  _fxCurrent = null;
  if (_fxRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(_fxRAF); _fxRAF = null; }
  if (_fxCanvas) {
    _fxCanvas.style.opacity = '0';
    setTimeout(function(){
      if (!_fxCurrent && _fxCtx) _fxCtx.clearRect(0,0,_fxCanvas.width,_fxCanvas.height);
    }, 800);
  }
  document.querySelectorAll('.fxb-btn').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('active'); });
}

var FX_EFFECTS = {

  // 🌧 Rain
  rain: function(cv,ctx) {
    var drops = Array.from({length:200},function(){
      return {x:Math.random()*cv.width,y:Math.random()*cv.height,l:10+Math.random()*20,s:4+Math.random()*8,a:0.2+Math.random()*0.4};
    });
    return function() {
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(4,8,20,0.25)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(140,180,255,0.5)'; ctx.lineWidth=1;
      drops.forEach(function(d){
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(d.x,d.y); ctx.lineTo(d.x-1,d.y+d.l);
        ctx.globalAlpha=d.a; ctx.stroke(); ctx.globalAlpha=1;
        d.y+=d.s;
        if(d.y>cv.height){d.y=-d.l;d.x=Math.random()*cv.width;}
      });
    };
  },

  // ⛈ Thunder Storm
  thunder: function(cv,ctx) {
    var drops = Array.from({length:300},function(){
      return {x:Math.random()*cv.width,y:Math.random()*cv.height,l:15+Math.random()*30,s:8+Math.random()*12,a:0.3+Math.random()*0.4};
    });
    var flash=0, flashTimer=0, nextFlash=Math.random()*180+60;
    return function() {
      // Dark stormy sky
      ctx.fillStyle=flash>0?'rgba(200,220,255,'+Math.min(0.15,flash*0.03)+')':'rgba(2,4,12,0.3)';
      ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      // Rain
      ctx.lineWidth=1.2;
      drops.forEach(function(d){
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(d.x,d.y); ctx.lineTo(d.x-2,d.y+d.l);
        ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(160,200,255,'+(d.a+(flash>0?0.3:0))+')';
        ctx.stroke();
        d.y+=d.s; if(d.y>cv.height){d.y=-d.l;d.x=Math.random()*cv.width;}
      });
      // Lightning
      flashTimer++;
      if(flash>0){ flash--; }
      if(flashTimer>nextFlash) {
        flash=8+Math.floor(Math.random()*6);
        flashTimer=0; nextFlash=Math.random()*200+80;
        // Draw bolt
        var bx=cv.width*0.2+Math.random()*cv.width*0.6, by=0;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(bx,by);
        var segs=8;
        for(var i=0;i<segs;i++){
          bx+=(Math.random()-0.5)*80; by+=cv.height/segs;
          ctx.lineTo(bx,by);
        }
        ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,220,0.9)'; ctx.lineWidth=2;
        ctx.shadowColor='#ffffaa'; ctx.shadowBlur=20; ctx.stroke();
        ctx.lineWidth=6; ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,220,0.2)'; ctx.stroke();
        ctx.shadowBlur=0;
      }
    };
  },

  // 🟩 Matrix
  matrix: function(cv,ctx) {
    var cols=Math.floor(cv.width/16);
    var drops=Array.from({length:cols},function(){return Math.random()*-cv.height;});
    var chars='0123456789ABCDEFアイウエオカキクケコサシスセソタチツテトナニ';
    return function() {
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.07)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      ctx.font='14px monospace';
      for(var i=0;i<drops.length;i++){
        var ch=chars[Math.floor(Math.random()*chars.length)];
        var bright=drops[i]<50?1:Math.max(0.15,1-drops[i]/cv.height);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,'+(Math.floor(180+bright*75))+','+Math.floor(bright*60)+','+(0.5+bright*0.5)+')';
        ctx.fillText(ch,i*16+4,drops[i]);
        drops[i]+=14;
        if(drops[i]>cv.height&&Math.random()>0.975)drops[i]=0;
      }
    };
  },

  // 📺 Glitch
  glitch: function(cv,ctx) {
    var t=0;
    return function() {
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.1)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      t++;
      if(Math.random()<0.06){
        var slices=3+Math.floor(Math.random()*7);
        for(var i=0;i<slices;i++){
          var sy=Math.floor(Math.random()*cv.height);
          var sh=Math.floor(2+Math.random()*24);
          var sx=Math.floor((Math.random()-0.5)*80);
          if(sy+sh<=cv.height&&Math.abs(sx)>2){
            var img=ctx.getImageData(0,sy,cv.width,sh);
            ctx.putImageData(img,sx,sy);
            // Color fringe
            var r=Math.random()<0.5;
            ctx.fillStyle=r?'rgba(255,0,60,0.08)':'rgba(0,200,255,0.08)';
            ctx.fillRect(0,sy,cv.width,sh);
          }
        }
      }
      // Scanlines
      for(var y=0;y<cv.height;y+=3){ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.03)';ctx.fillRect(0,y,cv.width,1);}
      // Occasional full flash
      if(Math.random()<0.005){ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,0,80,0.05)';ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);}
    };
  },

  // ❄️ Snow
  snow: function(cv,ctx) {
    var flakes=Array.from({length:180},function(){
      return {x:Math.random()*cv.width,y:Math.random()*cv.height,r:1+Math.random()*3,s:0.5+Math.random()*1.5,w:Math.random()*Math.PI*2,a:0.4+Math.random()*0.5};
    });
    var t=0;
    return function() {
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(5,8,20,0.2)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      t+=0.01;
      flakes.forEach(function(f,i){
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(f.x,f.y,f.r,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(220,235,255,'+f.a+')'; ctx.fill();
        f.y+=f.s; f.x+=Math.sin(t+f.w)*0.5;
        if(f.y>cv.height){f.y=-5;f.x=Math.random()*cv.width;}
        if(f.x<0)f.x=cv.width; if(f.x>cv.width)f.x=0;
      });
    };
  },

  // 🔥 Fire
  fire: function(cv,ctx) {
    var embers=Array.from({length:120},function(){
      return {x:Math.random()*cv.width,y:cv.height+20,vy:-(1+Math.random()*3),vx:(Math.random()-0.5),r:1+Math.random()*4,life:Math.random(),hue:15+Math.random()*25,a:0.8+Math.random()*0.2};
    });
    var t=0;
    return function() {
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      t+=0.02;
      embers.forEach(function(e,i){
        e.x+=e.vx+Math.sin(t+i*0.3)*0.4; e.y+=e.vy; e.life-=0.008;
        if(e.life<=0||e.y<-10){e.x=Math.random()*cv.width;e.y=cv.height+10;e.life=0.7+Math.random()*0.3;e.vy=-(1+Math.random()*3);}
        var g=ctx.createRadialGradient(e.x,e.y,0,e.x,e.y,e.r*4);
        g.addColorStop(0,'hsla('+e.hue+',100%,70%,'+e.life+')');
        g.addColorStop(0.5,'hsla('+e.hue+',100%,45%,'+(e.life*0.5)+')');
        g.addColorStop(1,'hsla('+e.hue+',100%,20%,0)');
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(e.x,e.y,e.r*4,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fill();
      });
    };
  },

  // 🌌 Space
  space: function(cv,ctx) {
    var stars=Array.from({length:200},function(){
      return {x:Math.random()*cv.width,y:Math.random()*cv.height,r:Math.random()*1.5,s:0.3+Math.random()*1.5,a:Math.random()*Math.PI*2};
    });
    var nebulas=[
      {x:cv.width*0.3,y:cv.height*0.4,hue:260,r:200},
      {x:cv.width*0.7,y:cv.height*0.6,hue:180,r:150},
    ];
    var t=0;
    return function() {
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,4,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      t+=0.008;
      // Nebula blobs
      nebulas.forEach(function(n){
        var g=ctx.createRadialGradient(n.x,n.y,0,n.x,n.y,n.r*(1+Math.sin(t)*0.1));
        g.addColorStop(0,'hsla('+n.hue+',80%,40%,0.04)');
        g.addColorStop(0.5,'hsla('+n.hue+',70%,30%,0.02)');
        g.addColorStop(1,'transparent');
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(n.x,n.y,n.r,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fill();
      });
      // Stars
      stars.forEach(function(s){
        s.a+=0.02; var twinkle=Math.sin(s.a)*0.4+0.6;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(s.x,s.y,s.r*twinkle,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(220,230,255,'+(0.5*twinkle)+')'; ctx.fill();
        // Shooting stars (rare)
        if(Math.random()<0.0003){
          var sx=Math.random()*cv.width,sy=Math.random()*cv.height*0.5;
          ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(sx,sy); ctx.lineTo(sx+120,sy+40);
          ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.6)'; ctx.lineWidth=1; ctx.stroke();
        }
      });
    };
  },

  // 🌈 Aurora
  aurora: function(cv,ctx) {
    var t=0;
    var bands=[
      {hue:160,y:cv.height*0.3,amp:80,speed:0.8},
      {hue:200,y:cv.height*0.45,amp:60,speed:1.1},
      {hue:280,y:cv.height*0.2,amp:100,speed:0.6},
    ];
    return function() {
      ctx.clearRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      t+=0.006;
      bands.forEach(function(b,bi){
        ctx.beginPath();
        for(var x=0;x<=cv.width;x+=4){
          var y=b.y+Math.sin(x*0.003+t*b.speed)*b.amp+Math.sin(x*0.007+t*0.7)*25;
          x===0?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);
        }
        ctx.lineTo(cv.width,cv.height); ctx.lineTo(0,cv.height); ctx.closePath();
        var g=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,cv.height);
        g.addColorStop(0,'transparent');
        g.addColorStop(0.3,'hsla('+(b.hue+bi*30)+',90%,60%,0.09)');
        g.addColorStop(0.5,'hsla('+(b.hue+bi*30)+',80%,70%,0.14)');
        g.addColorStop(0.7,'hsla('+(b.hue+bi*30)+',90%,60%,0.07)');
        g.addColorStop(1,'transparent');
        ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fill();
      });
    };
  },
};

// ── PLAYER LEVEL SYSTEM ──────────────────────────────────────
var LEVELS = [
  { id:'rookie',    name:'Rookie',    xp:0,    icon:'🌱', emoji:'🌱' },
  { id:'spark',     name:'Spark',     xp:500,  icon:'⚡', emoji:'⚡' },
  { id:'nova',      name:'Nova',      xp:2000, icon:'🌟', emoji:'🌟' },
  { id:'supernova', name:'Supernova', xp:6000, icon:'💥', emoji:'💥' },
  { id:'cosmic',    name:'Cosmic',    xp:15000,icon:'✨', emoji:'✨' },
];

var _xp = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('gv_xp') || '0');

function getLevel() {
  var lv = LEVELS[0];
  for (var i = 0; i < LEVELS.length; i++) {
    if (_xp >= LEVELS[i].xp) lv = LEVELS[i];
  }
  return lv;
}

function getNextLevel() {
  var lv = getLevel();
  var idx = LEVELS.findIndex(function(l){ return l.id === lv.id; });
  return idx < LEVELS.length - 1 ? LEVELS[idx + 1] : null;
}

function addXP(amount) {
  var oldLevel = getLevel();
  _xp += amount;
  localStorage.setItem('gv_xp', _xp);
  var newLevel = getLevel();

  if (newLevel.id !== oldLevel.id) {
    // Level up!
    setTimeout(function() {
      spawnParticles(['⭐','✨','💫','🌟'], 20);
      showToast(newLevel.emoji + ' Level Up! You are now ' + newLevel.name + '!', { icon: newLevel.emoji });
    }, 300);
  }
  updateLevelUI();
}

function updateLevelUI() {
  var lv   = getLevel();
  var next = getNextLevel();

  // XP progress
  var xpInLevel  = _xp - lv.xp;
  var xpNeeded   = next ? (next.xp - lv.xp) : 1;
  var pct        = next ? Math.min(100, Math.round(xpInLevel / xpNeeded * 100)) : 100;

  // Update badge in profile modal
  var badge = document.getElementById('level-badge');
  if (badge) {
    badge.className = 'level-badge level-' + lv.id;
    badge.innerHTML = lv.emoji + ' ' + lv.name;
  }

  // Update XP bar
  var fill  = document.getElementById('level-xp-fill');
  var label = document.getElementById('level-xp-label');
  var prog  = document.getElementById('level-xp-progress');
  if (fill)  { fill.style.width = pct + '%'; fill.className = 'xp-bar-fill ' + lv.id; }
  if (label) label.textContent = lv.name + (next ? ' → ' + next.name : ' (MAX)');
  if (prog)  prog.textContent = next ? (_xp.toLocaleString() + ' / ' + next.xp.toLocaleString() + ' XP') : 'MAX LEVEL';

  // Apply avatar ring to both nav avatar and profile avatar
  var ringClass = 'lvl-ring-' + lv.id;
  ['account-avatar','profile-big-avatar'].forEach(function(id) {
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    // Remove old ring classes
    el.classList.forEach(function(c) { if (c.startsWith('lvl-ring-')) el.classList.remove(c); });
    el.classList.add(ringClass);
  });

  // Show level badge next to username in nav
  var navLvl = document.getElementById('nav-level-badge');
  if (navLvl) {
    navLvl.className = 'level-badge level-' + lv.id;
    navLvl.textContent = lv.emoji;
    navLvl.style.padding = '2px 6px';
    navLvl.style.fontSize = '11px';
  }
  // Update rank+streak pill
  updateRankStreakPill();
}

function updateRankStreakPill() {
  var pill = document.getElementById('rank-streak-pill');
  var icon = document.getElementById('pill-level-icon');
  var name = document.getElementById('pill-level-name');
  var si   = document.getElementById('pill-streak-icon');
  var sc   = document.getElementById('pill-streak-count');
  if (!pill) return;
  var lv = getLevel();
  if (icon) icon.textContent = lv.emoji;
  if (name) { name.textContent = lv.name; }
  // Streak
  var streak = _streak || 0;
  if (sc) sc.textContent = streak + 'd';
  // Pick streak icon based on tier
  var sIcon = streak >= 10 ? '✨' : streak >= 5 ? '🔥' : streak >= 3 ? '🔥' : '🔥';
  if (si) si.textContent = sIcon;
  // Show if user has username
  pill.style.display = (currentUser && currentUser.username) ? 'flex' : 'none';
}

// ── PROGRESS MODAL ───────────────────────────────────────────
function openProgressModal() {
  var overlay = document.getElementById('progress-modal-overlay');
  if (overlay) { overlay.classList.add('open'); renderProgressModal(); }
}
function closeProgressModal() {
  var overlay = document.getElementById('progress-modal-overlay');
  if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove('open');
}

function renderProgressModal() {
  var lv   = getLevel();
  var next = getNextLevel();
  var xpInLevel = _xp - lv.xp;
  var xpNeeded  = next ? next.xp - lv.xp : 1;
  var pct       = next ? Math.min(100, Math.round(xpInLevel / xpNeeded * 100)) : 100;

  // Level icon
  var icon = document.getElementById('pm-level-icon');
  if (icon) icon.textContent = lv.emoji;

  // Level badge
  var badge = document.getElementById('pm-level-badge');
  if (badge) { badge.className = 'level-badge level-' + lv.id; badge.innerHTML = lv.emoji + ' ' + lv.name; }

  // XP fill
  var fill = document.getElementById('pm-xp-fill');
  if (fill) { fill.style.width = pct + '%'; fill.className = 'xp-bar-fill ' + lv.id; }

  // XP labels
  var total = document.getElementById('pm-xp-total');
  if (total) total.textContent = _xp.toLocaleString() + ' XP total';

  var lbl = document.getElementById('pm-xp-label');
  if (lbl) lbl.textContent = next
    ? (xpInLevel.toLocaleString() + ' / ' + xpNeeded.toLocaleString() + ' XP to ' + next.name)
    : 'MAX LEVEL REACHED';

  // Level journey nodes
  var nodes = document.getElementById('pm-all-levels');
  if (nodes) {
    nodes.innerHTML = LEVELS.map(function(l) {
      var reached  = _xp >= l.xp;
      var isCurrent = l.id === lv.id;
      return '<div class="pm-level-node' + (reached?' reached':'') + (isCurrent?' current':'') + '" style="'
        + (isCurrent ? 'border-color:rgba(255,255,255,0.4);background:rgba(255,255,255,0.1);' : '')
        + '">' + l.emoji + ' ' + l.name
        + (isCurrent ? ' ←' : '')
        + '</div>';
    }).join('');
  }

  // Streak
  var days = _streak || 0;
  var tier = getStreakTier(days);
  var sd = document.getElementById('pm-streak-days');
  if (sd) sd.innerHTML = days + ' <span style="font-size:16px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.5);">day' + (days !== 1 ? 's' : '') + '</span>';
  var st = document.getElementById('pm-streak-tier');
  if (st) st.textContent = tier ? (tier.emoji + ' ' + tier.label + ' Streak') : (days > 0 ? 'Keep going!' : 'Play daily to build your streak');
  var se = document.getElementById('pm-streak-emoji');
  if (se) se.textContent = tier ? tier.emoji.split('')[0] : '🔥';
  var xm = document.getElementById('pm-xp-mult');
  if (xm) xm.textContent = (_streakXP || 1.0).toFixed(1) + '×';

  // Streak milestones
  var ms = document.getElementById('pm-streak-milestones');
  if (ms) {
    ms.innerHTML = [1,3,5,7,10,14,21].map(function(d) {
      var reached = days >= d;
      var t = getStreakTier(d);
      return '<div style="padding:4px 10px;border-radius:20px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;'
        + 'border:1px solid ' + (reached ? 'rgba(245,158,11,0.4)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.07)') + ';'
        + 'background:' + (reached ? 'rgba(245,158,11,0.1)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)') + ';'
        + 'color:' + (reached ? '#f59e0b' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)') + ';">'
        + (t ? t.emoji.split('')[0] + ' ' : '') + d + 'd'
        + '</div>';
    }).join('');
  }

  // Stats
  var sp = document.getElementById('pm-stat-played');
  if (sp) sp.textContent = (recent ? recent.length : 0) + (achStats && achStats.played ? achStats.played : 0);
  var sw = document.getElementById('pm-stat-wins');
  if (sw) sw.textContent = (_csSession ? _csSession.won : 0);
  var sc2 = document.getElementById('pm-stat-coins');
  if (sc2) sc2.textContent = stormCoins.toLocaleString();
}


// ── CRASH AUTO BET ────────────────────────────────────────────
var _crashAutoRunning=false, _crashAutoBetsLeft=0;

function startCrashAuto(){
  if(_crashAutoRunning)return;
  var numBets=parseInt(document.getElementById('crash-num-bets').value)||10;
  _crashAutoBetsLeft=numBets;
  _crashAutoRunning=true;
  var startBtn=document.getElementById('crash-auto-start');
  var stopBtn=document.getElementById('crash-auto-stop');
  if(startBtn)startBtn.style.display='none';
  if(stopBtn)stopBtn.style.display='block';
  runNextAutoCrash();
}

function stopCrashAuto(){
  _crashAutoRunning=false;
  _crashAutoBetsLeft=0;
  var startBtn=document.getElementById('crash-auto-start');
  var stopBtn=document.getElementById('crash-auto-stop');
  if(startBtn)startBtn.style.display='block';
  if(stopBtn)stopBtn.style.display='none';
}

function runNextAutoCrash(){
  if(!_crashAutoRunning||_crashAutoBetsLeft<=0){stopCrashAuto();return;}
  _crashAutoBetsLeft--;
  // Trigger a crash bet using current settings
  var bet=getBet('crash-bet'); if(!bet||bet>stormCoins){stopCrashAuto();showToast('Auto stopped — not enough coins');return;}
  updateCoins(-bet);crashBet=bet;crashMultiplier=1.0;crashCashedOut=false;crashRunning=true;
  var r=Math.random();
  crashTarget=r<0.05?1.05+Math.random()*0.5:Math.max(1.1,(1/(1-Math.random()*0.97)));
  var autoCashout=parseFloat(document.getElementById('crash-auto').value)||2.0;
  crashPoints=[];
  if(!crashCanvas){crashCanvas=document.getElementById('crash-canvas');if(crashCanvas)crashCtx=crashCanvas.getContext('2d');}
  clearTimeout(crashInterval);
  function autoTick(){
    if(!crashRunning)return;
    crashMultiplier+=0.02+crashMultiplier*0.004;
    crashPoints.push(parseFloat(crashMultiplier.toFixed(3)));
    var coEl=document.getElementById('crash-co-mult');if(coEl)coEl.textContent=crashMultiplier.toFixed(2)+'×';
    drawCrashChart(false);
    if(crashMultiplier>=autoCashout&&!crashCashedOut){
      // Auto cash out
      crashCashedOut=true;crashRunning=false;
      var prize=crashBet*crashMultiplier;updateCoins(prize);
      drawCrashChart(false);
      addLiveBet('You','Crash',crashBet,prize-crashBet);
      crashHistory.unshift(crashMultiplier.toFixed(2)+'×');
      if(crashHistory.length>8)crashHistory.pop();renderCrashHist();
      setTimeout(function(){if(_crashAutoRunning)runNextAutoCrash();},1200);
      return;
    }
    if(crashMultiplier>=crashTarget){
      crashRunning=false;drawCrashChart(true);
      addLiveBet('You','Crash',crashBet,-crashBet);
      crashHistory.unshift(crashTarget.toFixed(2)+'×');
      if(crashHistory.length>8)crashHistory.pop();renderCrashHist();
      setTimeout(function(){if(_crashAutoRunning)runNextAutoCrash();},1200);
      return;
    }
    crashInterval=setTimeout(autoTick,50);
  }
  autoTick();
}

// ── MINES AUTO TAB (simple auto — picks random tiles automatically) ──
var _minesAutoRunning=false;

function minesSetTab(tab){
  var m=document.getElementById('mines-tab-manual'), a=document.getElementById('mines-tab-auto');
  if(m){m.style.background=tab==='manual'?'#1f6feb':'transparent';m.style.color=tab==='manual'?'#fff':'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)';}
  if(a){a.style.background=tab==='auto'?'#1f6feb':'transparent';a.style.color=tab==='auto'?'#fff':'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)';}
  var mf=document.getElementById('mines-manual-actions'), af=document.getElementById('mines-auto-actions');
  if(mf)mf.style.display=tab==='auto'?'none':'flex';
  if(af)af.style.display=tab==='auto'?'flex':'none';
}

function startMinesAuto(){
  if(_minesAutoRunning||minesActive)return;
  _minesAutoRunning=true;
  var autoBtn=document.getElementById('mines-auto-start');
  var stopBtn=document.getElementById('mines-auto-stop');
  if(autoBtn)autoBtn.style.display='none';
  if(stopBtn)stopBtn.style.display='block';
  runMinesAutoRound();
}

function stopMinesAuto(){
  _minesAutoRunning=false;
  if(minesActive)cashoutMines();
  var autoBtn=document.getElementById('mines-auto-start');
  var stopBtn=document.getElementById('mines-auto-stop');
  if(autoBtn)autoBtn.style.display='block';
  if(stopBtn)stopBtn.style.display='none';
}

function runMinesAutoRound(){
  if(!_minesAutoRunning){stopMinesAuto();return;}
  var bet=parseInt(document.getElementById('mines-bet').value)||10;
  if(bet>stormCoins){stopMinesAuto();showToast('Auto stopped — not enough coins');return;}
  startMines();
  // Auto-pick tiles up to cashout target
  var targetMult=parseFloat(document.getElementById('mines-auto-target').value)||1.5;
  function autoPick(){
    if(!minesActive||!_minesAutoRunning){
      setTimeout(function(){if(_minesAutoRunning)runMinesAutoRound();},800);
      return;
    }
    var mt=MINES_MULT[minesMineCount]||MINES_MULT[5];
    var currM=mt[Math.min(minesSafeCount,mt.length-1)]||1;
    if(currM>=targetMult){cashoutMines();setTimeout(function(){if(_minesAutoRunning)runMinesAutoRound();},800);return;}
    pickRandomMine();
    setTimeout(autoPick,400);
  }
  setTimeout(autoPick,300);
}

// ── MUSIC PLAYER ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// ── DAILY SPIN WHEEL ─────────────────────────────────────────
var SPIN_PRIZES = [
  { label:'+50',    coins:50,   color:'#7c3aed', emoji:'⚡', type:'coins'   },
  { label:'+100',   coins:100,  color:'#2563eb', emoji:'⚡', type:'coins'   },
  { label:'+200',   coins:200,  color:'#059669', emoji:'⚡', type:'coins'   },
  { label:'+500',   coins:500,  color:'#d97706', emoji:'⚡', type:'coins'   },
  { label:'+25',    coins:25,   color:'#9d174d', emoji:'⚡', type:'coins'   },
  { label:'JACKPOT',coins:2000, color:'#b45309', emoji:'🏆', type:'jackpot' },
  { label:'+75',    coins:75,   color:'#0e7490', emoji:'⚡', type:'coins'   },
  { label:'x2 NEXT',coins:0,   color:'#4338ca', emoji:'🌟', type:'x2'      },
];
var _spinAngle      = 0;
var _spinning       = false;
var _spinCanDrawn   = false;

function getSpinKey() { return 'gv_spin_' + new Date().toDateString().replace(/ /g,'_'); }

function canSpin() {
  return !localStorage.getItem(getSpinKey());
}

function drawWheel(angle) {
  var canvas = document.getElementById('spin-wheel-modal');
  if (!canvas) return;
  var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  var W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;
  var cx = W/2, cy = H/2, r = W/2 - 4;
  var slices = SPIN_PRIZES.length;
  var arc = (Math.PI * 2) / slices;

  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

  // Outer ring shadow
  ctx.save();
  ctx.shadowColor = 'rgba(124,58,237,0.4)';
  ctx.shadowBlur  = 18;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(cx, cy, r+3, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)';
  ctx.lineWidth   = 2;
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();

  SPIN_PRIZES.forEach(function(p, i) {
    var startAngle = angle + i * arc;
    var endAngle   = startAngle + arc;

    // Slice fill
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(cx, cy);
    ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, startAngle, endAngle);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
    ctx.fill();

    // Slice border
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(cx, cy);
    ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, startAngle, endAngle);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)';
    ctx.lineWidth   = 1.5;
    ctx.stroke();

    // Label
    ctx.save();
    ctx.translate(cx, cy);
    ctx.rotate(startAngle + arc/2);
    ctx.textAlign    = 'right';
    ctx.fillStyle    = '#fff';
    ctx.font         = 'bold 12px Outfit, sans-serif';
    ctx.shadowColor  = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)';
    ctx.shadowBlur   = 3;
    ctx.fillText(p.emoji + ' ' + p.label, r - 10, 4);
    ctx.restore();
  });

  // Center hub
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(cx, cy, 18, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#0d0d12';
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)';
  ctx.lineWidth   = 2;
  ctx.stroke();

  // Center dot
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(cx, cy, 6, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.7)';
  ctx.fill();
}

function buildSpinPrizesList() {
  var el = document.getElementById('spin-prizes-list');
  if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = SPIN_PRIZES.map(function(p) {
    return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.03);'
      + 'border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06);border-radius:8px;padding:4px 10px;">'
      + '<div style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:' + p.color + ';flex-shrink:0;"></div>'
      + '<span style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.55);">' + p.emoji + ' ' + p.label + '</span>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}


function openSpinModal() {
  var overlay = document.getElementById('spin-modal-overlay');
  if (overlay) overlay.classList.add('open');
  // Re-draw wheel in modal size
  drawWheel(_spinAngle);
}
function closeSpinModal() {
  var overlay = document.getElementById('spin-modal-overlay');
  if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove('open');
}

function initSpinWheel() {
  drawWheel(0);
  buildSpinPrizesList();
  updateSpinUI();
  // Idle drift animation
  var driftAngle = 0;
  function drift() {
    if (!_spinning) {
      driftAngle += 0.003;
      drawWheel(driftAngle);
      _spinAngle = driftAngle;
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(drift);
  }
  drift();
}

function updateSpinUI() {
  var dot = document.getElementById('spin-float-dot');
  if (dot) dot.className = canSpin() ? 'spin-dot' : 'spin-dot used';
  var btn    = document.getElementById('spin-btn');
  var badge  = document.getElementById('spin-status-badge');
  var cdTxt  = document.getElementById('spin-cooldown-txt');
  if (!canSpin()) {
    if (btn)   { btn.disabled = true; btn.style.opacity = '0.4'; btn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed'; btn.textContent = '⏳ Come back tomorrow'; }
    if (badge) { badge.textContent = 'USED'; badge.style.color = 'var(--muted)'; badge.style.borderColor = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'; badge.style.background = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)'; }
    if (cdTxt) { cdTxt.style.display = 'block'; startSpinCooldownTimer(); }
  } else {
    if (btn)   { btn.disabled = false; btn.style.opacity = '1'; btn.style.cursor = 'pointer'; btn.textContent = '🎡 SPIN NOW'; }
    if (badge) { badge.textContent = 'AVAILABLE'; badge.style.color = '#4ade80'; badge.style.borderColor = 'rgba(74,222,128,0.25)'; badge.style.background = 'rgba(74,222,128,0.1)'; }
    if (cdTxt) cdTxt.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

function startSpinCooldownTimer() {
  function tick() {
    var el = document.getElementById('spin-cooldown-txt');
    if (!el) return;
    var now      = new Date();
    var midnight = new Date(now); midnight.setHours(24,0,0,0);
    var diff     = midnight - now;
    var h = Math.floor(diff/3600000);
    var m = Math.floor((diff%3600000)/60000);
    var s = Math.floor((diff%60000)/1000);
    el.textContent = 'Next spin in ' + String(h).padStart(2,'0') + ':' + String(m).padStart(2,'0') + ':' + String(s).padStart(2,'0');
    if (canSpin()) { updateSpinUI(); return; }
    setTimeout(tick, 1000);
  }
  tick();
}

function triggerSpin() {
  if (_spinning || !canSpin()) return;
  _spinning = true;

  var btn = document.getElementById('spin-btn');
  if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Spinning...'; }

  // Pick random prize
  var prizeIdx = Math.floor(Math.random() * SPIN_PRIZES.length);
  var prize    = SPIN_PRIZES[prizeIdx];

  // Calculate target angle — land prize at top (pointer = -PI/2)
  var slices   = SPIN_PRIZES.length;
  var arc      = (Math.PI * 2) / slices;
  // Extra full rotations for drama
  var extraRot = (5 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)) * Math.PI * 2;
  // Target: pointer at top = -PI/2, prize center should be at top
  var prizeCenter = prizeIdx * arc + arc/2;
  var targetAngle = extraRot + (-Math.PI/2 - prizeCenter);
  var startAngle  = _spinAngle;
  var duration    = 4500 + Math.random() * 1000;
  var startTime   = null;

  function easeOut(t) {
    return 1 - Math.pow(1 - t, 4);
  }

  function animFrame(ts) {
    if (!startTime) startTime = ts;
    var elapsed  = ts - startTime;
    var progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
    var eased    = easeOut(progress);
    var angle    = startAngle + (targetAngle - startAngle) * eased;

    _spinAngle = angle;
    drawWheel(angle);

    if (progress < 1) {
      requestAnimationFrame(animFrame);
    } else {
      // Done
      _spinning = false;
      localStorage.setItem(getSpinKey(), '1');
      showSpinResult(prize);
      updateSpinUI();
    }
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(animFrame);
}

function showSpinResult(prize) {
  var box = document.getElementById('spin-result-box');
  if (!box) return;

  if (prize.type === 'jackpot') {
    box.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:32px;margin-bottom:4px;">🏆</div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;font-size:28px;font-weight:900;color:#f59e0b;text-shadow:0 0 20px rgba(245,158,11,0.5);">JACKPOT!</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:13px;color:#4ade80;font-weight:700;margin-top:4px;">+⚡' + prize.coins + ' coins!</div>';
    updateCoins(prize.coins);
    if (typeof bumpCoins === 'function') bumpCoins();
    if (typeof spawnParticles === 'function') spawnParticles(['🏆','⚡','💰','🎉'], 20);
    showToast('🏆 JACKPOT! +⚡' + prize.coins, { icon:'🏆' });
  } else if (prize.type === 'x2') {
    box.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:32px;margin-bottom:4px;">🌟</div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;font-size:22px;font-weight:900;color:#818cf8;">DOUBLE NEXT WIN!</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:12px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.4);margin-top:4px;">Your next casino win is doubled</div>';
    localStorage.setItem('gv_x2_next', '1');
    showToast('🌟 Next win doubled!', { icon:'🌟' });
  } else {
    box.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:26px;margin-bottom:4px;">' + prize.emoji + '</div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;font-size:30px;font-weight:900;color:#4ade80;text-shadow:0 0 16px rgba(74,222,128,0.4);">+⚡' + prize.coins + '</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:12px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.4);margin-top:2px;">coins added to your balance</div>';
    updateCoins(prize.coins);
    if (typeof bumpCoins === 'function') bumpCoins();
    if (typeof spawnParticles === 'function') spawnParticles(['⚡','💰'], 10);
    showToast('🎡 You won +⚡' + prize.coins + '!', { icon:'🎡' });
  }
}

function hypeGenEvent() {
  var totalWeight = _hypeEvents.reduce(function(s,e){ return s+e.weight; }, 0);
  var r = Math.random() * totalWeight;
  var cum = 0;
  for (var i=0; i<_hypeEvents.length; i++) {
    cum += _hypeEvents[i].weight;
    if (r < cum) {
      var item = _hypeEvents[i].gen();
      return item;
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function timeAgo(ts) {
  var s = Math.floor((Date.now()-ts)/1000);
  if (s < 5)  return 'just now';
  if (s < 60) return s + 's ago';
  return Math.floor(s/60) + 'm ago';
}

function hypePush(item) {
  if (!item) return;
  item.ts = Date.now();
  _hypeItems.unshift(item);
  if (_hypeItems.length > 40) _hypeItems.pop();
  if (!_hypePaused) hypeRender();
  hypeUpdateStats();
}

function hypeRender() {
  var list = document.getElementById('hype-feed-list');
  if (!list) return;
  if (_hypeItems.length === 0) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:60px 20px;color:var(--muted);font-size:13px;">Warming up the feed…</div>';
    return;
  }
  list.innerHTML = _hypeItems.map(function(item) {
    return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;'
      + 'background:rgba(255,255,255,0.025);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.055);'
      + 'border-left:3px solid ' + item.color + ';'
      + 'border-radius:12px;padding:11px 14px;animation:fadeIn 0.3s ease both;">'
      + '<div style="font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0;">' + item.icon + '</div>'
      + '<div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">'
      +   '<div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.8);line-height:1.5;">' + item.text + '</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-end;gap:4px;flex-shrink:0;">'
      +   '<span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:1px;color:' + item.color + ';'
      +     'background:' + item.color + '18;border:1px solid ' + item.color + '33;'
      +     'border-radius:20px;padding:2px 7px;">' + item.badge + '</span>'
      +   '<span style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);">' + timeAgo(item.ts) + '</span>'
      + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function hypeUpdateStats() {
  var w = document.getElementById('hype-wins-today');
  var c = document.getElementById('hype-coins-today');
  var p = document.getElementById('hype-plays-today');
  if (w) w.textContent = _hypeWins;
  if (c) c.textContent = _hypeCoins >= 1000 ? (_hypeCoins/1000).toFixed(1)+'k' : _hypeCoins;
  if (p) p.textContent = _hypePlays;
}

function hypePause() {
  _hypePaused = !_hypePaused;
  var btn = document.getElementById('hype-pause-btn');
  if (btn) btn.textContent = _hypePaused ? '▶ Resume' : '⏸ Pause';
}

function hypeClear() {
  _hypeItems = [];
  _hypeWins = _hypeCoins = _hypePlays = 0;
  hypeRender();
  hypeUpdateStats();
}

function initHypeFeed() {
  // Seed with 8 initial events
  for (var i=0; i<8; i++) {
    var item = hypeGenEvent();
    if (item) { item.ts = Date.now() - (8-i)*22000; _hypeItems.push(item); }
  }
  hypeRender();
  hypeUpdateStats();
  // New event every 4-7 seconds
  function schedNext() {
    var delay = 4000 + Math.random()*3000;
    _hypeInterval = setTimeout(function() {
      hypePush(hypeGenEvent());
      schedNext();
    }, delay);
  }
  schedNext();
  // Refresh timestamps every 30s so "just now" ages correctly
  setInterval(function() {
    if (!_hypePaused) hypeRender();
  }, 30000);
}

// Also push real player events into hype feed
function hyeAddMyEvent(type, text, icon, color, badge) {
  hypePush({ icon:icon, color:color, badge:badge, text:text });
}

// ── RECENT WINS TICKER ───────────────────────────────────────
var _winsPool = [];
var _winNames = ['Storm_King','LuckyAce','NovaBolt','xX_Viper_Xx','GlitchGod',
  'CryptoFox','ZeroG','IronWolf','NeonRift','ShadowAce','BladeX','PixelPunk'];
var _winGames = [
  {n:'Crash',   emotes:['📈','🚀'],  range:[2,50]},
  {n:'Slots',   emotes:['🎰','💎'],  range:[5,200]},
  {n:'Blackjack',emotes:['🃏','♠️'], range:[2,10]},
  {n:'Roulette',emotes:['🎡','🔴'],  range:[2,36]},
  {n:'Plinko',  emotes:['🎯','⚡'],  range:[3,100]},
  {n:'Mines',   emotes:['💎','💣'],  range:[2,25]},
  {n:'Hi-Lo',   emotes:['🃏','🔮'],  range:[2,30]},
];

function genWinItem() {
  var name  = _winNames[Math.floor(Math.random() * _winNames.length)];
  var game  = _winGames[Math.floor(Math.random() * _winGames.length)];
  var emoji = game.emotes[Math.floor(Math.random() * game.emotes.length)];
  var mult  = (game.range[0] + Math.random() * (game.range[1] - game.range[0])).toFixed(1);
  var bet   = [10,25,50,100][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
  var prize = Math.round(bet * parseFloat(mult));
  return '<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;padding:8px 16px;border-right:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);font-size:12px;">'
    + '<span>' + emoji + '</span>'
    + '<span style="color:rgba(255,255,255,0.55);">' + name + '</span>'
    + '<span style="color:rgba(255,255,255,0.3);">won</span>'
    + '<span style="color:#4ade80;font-weight:700;font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;font-size:13px;">+⚡' + prize + '</span>'
    + '<span style="color:rgba(255,255,255,0.25);font-size:11px;">on ' + game.n + '</span>'
    + '<span style="color:rgba(245,158,11,0.6);font-size:10px;">' + mult + '×</span>'
    + '</span>';
}

function initWinsTicker() {
  var inner = document.getElementById('wins-ticker-inner');
  if (!inner) return;
  // Build 16 items, duplicate for seamless loop
  var items = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < 16; i++) items.push(genWinItem());
  var html = items.join('') + items.join(''); // duplicate
  inner.innerHTML = html;

  // Refresh with new wins every 30s
  setInterval(function() {
    var items2 = [];
    for (var j = 0; j < 16; j++) items2.push(genWinItem());
    inner.innerHTML = items2.join('') + items2.join('');
  }, 30000);
}

function saveQuickNotes(val) {
  localStorage.setItem('gv_notes', val);
  var cc = document.getElementById('notes-char-count');

}

  localStorage.removeItem('gv_notes');
  var ta = document.getElementById('quick-notes-area');
  if (ta) { ta.value = ''; }
  var cc = document.getElementById('notes-char-count');
  if (cc) cc.textContent = '0 / 1000';
}
function loadQuickNotes() {
  var ta = document.getElementById('quick-notes-area');
  if (!ta) return;
  var saved = localStorage.getItem('gv_notes') || '';
  ta.value = saved;
  var cc = document.getElementById('notes-char-count');
  if (cc) cc.textContent = saved.length + ' / 1000';
}

// ── CASINO LAST RESULT + SESSION STATS ───────────────────────
var _csSession = { played:0, won:0, lost:0, profit:0, streak:0, streakDir:'none' };

function updateCasinoLastResult(gameName, betAmt, resultAmt, mult) {
  var isWin = resultAmt > 0;
  var net   = resultAmt - betAmt;

  // Update session
  _csSession.played++;
  if (isWin) {
    _csSession.won++;
    _csSession.profit += net;
    _csSession.streak = _csSession.streakDir === 'win' ? _csSession.streak + 1 : 1;
    _csSession.streakDir = 'win';
  } else {
    _csSession.lost++;
    _csSession.profit += net;
    _csSession.streak = _csSession.streakDir === 'lose' ? _csSession.streak + 1 : 1;
    _csSession.streakDir = 'lose';
  }

  // Show last result panel
  var panel = document.getElementById('casino-last-result');
  if (!panel) return;

  var badge  = document.getElementById('lr-badge');
  var amount = document.getElementById('lr-amount');
  var meta   = document.getElementById('lr-meta');
  var odds   = document.getElementById('lr-odds');
  var sv     = document.getElementById('lr-streak-val');
  var sl     = document.getElementById('lr-streak-lbl');
  var gn     = document.getElementById('lr-game-name');

  var icon = { 'Crash':'📈','Lucky Slots':'🎰','Blackjack':'🃏','Roulette':'🎡',
    'Dice':'🎲','Coin Flip':'🪙','Plinko':'🎯','Mines':'💣',
    'Hi-Lo Cards':'🃏','CS Cases':'📦','Video Poker':'🃏','Baccarat':'🎴','Crossy Road':'🐸' };

  gn.textContent = (icon[gameName] || '🎮') + ' ' + gameName;
  badge.textContent  = isWin ? 'WIN' : 'LOSS';
  badge.className    = 'lr-result-badge ' + (isWin ? 'win' : 'lose');
  amount.textContent = (net >= 0 ? '+' : '') + '⚡' + Math.abs(net).toFixed(0);
  amount.className   = 'lr-amount ' + (isWin ? 'win' : 'lose');
  meta.textContent   = 'Bet ⚡' + betAmt.toFixed(0) + ' · Returned ⚡' + (isWin ? resultAmt.toFixed(0) : '0');
  odds.textContent   = mult ? mult.toFixed(2) + '×' : '—';

  var streakWord = _csSession.streakDir === 'win' ? '🔥 WIN' : '❄️ LOSE';
  sv.textContent = _csSession.streak + ((_csSession.streak > 1) ? (isWin ? ' 🔥' : ' ❄️') : '');
  sv.className   = 'lr-streak-val ' + (_csSession.streakDir === 'win' ? 'hot' : 'cold');
  sl.textContent = _csSession.streak > 1 ? 'STREAK' : 'LAST';

  panel.style.display = 'block';
  panel.style.animation = 'none';
  void panel.offsetWidth;
  panel.style.animation = 'lrSlideIn 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.22,1,0.36,1) both';

  // Update session bar
  var sp = document.getElementById('ss-played');
  var sw = document.getElementById('ss-won');
  var sl2 = document.getElementById('ss-lost');
  var pr = document.getElementById('ss-profit');
  var wr = document.getElementById('ss-winrate');
  if (sp) sp.textContent = _csSession.played;
  if (sw) sw.textContent = _csSession.won;
  if (sl2) sl2.textContent = _csSession.lost;
  if (pr) {
    var p = _csSession.profit;
    pr.textContent = (p >= 0 ? '+⚡' : '-⚡') + Math.abs(p).toFixed(0);
    pr.style.color = p >= 0 ? '#4ade80' : '#f87171';
  }
  if (wr) {
    var rate = _csSession.played > 0 ? Math.round((_csSession.won / _csSession.played)*100) : 0;
    wr.textContent = rate + '%';
    wr.style.color = rate >= 50 ? '#4ade80' : rate >= 35 ? '#f59e0b' : '#f87171';
  }
}

var DAILY_CHALLENGE_POOL = [

  { id:'win3_cas', icon:'🏆', name:'Win 3 Casino Games', desc:'Win any 3 casino games today',       goal:3,  stat:'casino_wins',reward:250 },
  { id:'bet500',   icon:'💸', name:'High Roller',        desc:'Bet a total of ⚡500+ today',        goal:500,stat:'total_bet',   reward:200 },
  { id:'lib2',     icon:'📚', name:'Add 2 to Library',   desc:'Add 2 games to your library',        goal:2,  stat:'lib_adds',   reward:80  },
  { id:'crash10',  icon:'📈', name:'Survive Crash 10×',  desc:'Cash out at 10× or higher in Crash', goal:1,  stat:'crash10',    reward:300 },
  { id:'slots_win',icon:'🎰', name:'Slots Winner',       desc:'Win on Lucky Slots',                 goal:1,  stat:'slots_win',  reward:120 },
  { id:'play_hor', icon:'👻', name:'Horror Fan',         desc:'Play a Horror game today',           goal:1,  stat:'horror_play', reward:60 },
  { id:'bj_win',   icon:'🃏', name:'Beat the Dealer',    desc:'Win a hand of Blackjack',            goal:1,  stat:'bj_win',     reward:150 },
  { id:'netpos',   icon:'📊', name:'Stay Profitable',    desc:'End the session with +coins',        goal:1,  stat:'net_positive',reward:175 },
  { id:'plinko3',  icon:'🎯', name:'Plinko x3',          desc:'Play Plinko 3 times',                goal:3,  stat:'plinko_play', reward:90 },
];

var _dcProgress = {};
var _dcClaimed  = {};
var _dcToday    = [];

function getDCKey() { return 'gv_dc_' + new Date().toDateString().replace(/ /g,'_'); }
function loadDC() {
  var k = getDCKey();
  var saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(k) || 'null');
  if (saved) {
    _dcToday    = saved.challenges;
    _dcProgress = saved.progress || {};
    _dcClaimed  = saved.claimed  || {};
  } else {
    // Pick 3 random challenges for today using date as seed
    var seed = new Date().toDateString();
    var pool = DAILY_CHALLENGE_POOL.slice();
    pool.sort(function(a,b){ return (seed+a.id).length - (seed+b.id).length || a.id.localeCompare(b.id); });
    _dcToday    = pool.slice(0,3);
    _dcProgress = {};
    _dcClaimed  = {};
    saveDC();
  }
}
function saveDC() {
  var k = getDCKey();
  localStorage.setItem(k, JSON.stringify({ challenges:_dcToday, progress:_dcProgress, claimed:_dcClaimed }));
}

function trackDC(stat, amount) {
  amount = amount || 1;
  var changed = false;
  _dcToday.forEach(function(c) {
    if (c.stat === stat) {
      _dcProgress[c.id] = Math.min(c.goal, (_dcProgress[c.id]||0) + amount);
      changed = true;
    }
  });
  if (changed) { saveDC(); renderDC(); }
}

function claimDC(id) {
  var c = _dcToday.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
  if (!c || _dcClaimed[id]) return;
  if ((_dcProgress[id]||0) < c.goal) return;
  _dcClaimed[id] = true;
  updateCoins(c.reward);
  bumpCoins();
  saveDC();
  renderDC();
  spawnParticles(['⚡','🏆','💰'], 8);
  showToast('Challenge complete! +⚡' + c.reward, { type:'t-coin', icon:'🏆' });
}

function renderDC() {
  var grid = document.getElementById('daily-challenges-grid');
  if (!grid) return;
  grid.innerHTML = _dcToday.map(function(c) {
    var prog    = _dcProgress[c.id] || 0;
    var pct     = Math.min(100, Math.round((prog / c.goal) * 100));
    var done    = prog >= c.goal;
    var claimed = !!_dcClaimed[c.id];
    var btn = '';
    if (claimed) {
      btn = '<div class="challenge-done-badge">&#x2705;</div>';
    } else if (done) {
      btn = '<button class="challenge-claim-btn" onclick="claimDC(\'' + c.id + '\')">Claim!</button>';
    }
    return '<div class="challenge-card' + (claimed ? ' completed' : '') + '">'
      + '<div class="challenge-icon">' + c.icon + '</div>'
      + '<div class="challenge-body">'
      +   '<div class="challenge-name">' + c.name + '</div>'
      +   '<div class="challenge-desc">' + c.desc + '</div>'
      +   '<div class="challenge-progress-bar"><div class="challenge-progress-fill" style="width:' + pct + '%"></div></div>'
      +   '<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--muted);margin-top:4px;">' + prog + ' / ' + c.goal + '</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + '<div class="challenge-reward">'
      +   '<div class="challenge-reward-val">&#x26A1;' + c.reward + '</div>'
      +   '<div class="challenge-reward-lbl">reward</div>'
      +   btn
      + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function startChallengeTimer() {
  function update() {
    var el = document.getElementById('challenge-timer');
    if (!el) return;
    var now      = new Date();
    var midnight = new Date(now); midnight.setHours(24,0,0,0);
    var diff     = midnight - now;
    var h = Math.floor(diff/3600000);
    var m = Math.floor((diff%3600000)/60000);
    var s = Math.floor((diff%60000)/1000);
    el.textContent = String(h).padStart(2,'0') + ':' + String(m).padStart(2,'0') + ':' + String(s).padStart(2,'0');
  }
  update();
  setInterval(update, 1000);
}

// ── LEADERBOARD ───────────────────────────────────────────────
var _lbTab = 'coins';
var _lbData = null;

// Fake realistic players seeded from today's date
function getLBPlayers() {
  var names = ['xX_Apex_Xx','NovaKing','CryptoGhost','LuckyDucky','ZeroCool',
    'ShadowFox','NeonRift','BladeRunner','StormChaser','PixelPunk',
    'VoidWalker','GlitchKing','NightOwl','IronFist','CyberWolf'];
  var seed = new Date().toDateString();
  var hash = function(s){ var h=0; for(var i=0;i<s.length;i++)h=(h*31+s.charCodeAt(i))|0; return Math.abs(h); };
  return names.map(function(n,i){
    var h = hash(seed+n);
    return {
      name:   n,
      coins:  5000 + (h % 95000),
      wins:   20  + (hash(seed+n+'w') % 480),
      played: 30  + (hash(seed+n+'p') % 970),
      avatar: n[0].toUpperCase()
    };
  }).sort(function(a,b){ return b.coins - a.coins; });
}

function lbSetTab(tab) {
  _lbTab = tab;
  ['coins','wins','played'].forEach(function(t){
    var btn = document.getElementById('lb-tab-'+t);
    if(btn) btn.classList.toggle('active', t===tab);
  });
  renderLB();
}

function renderLB() {
  var list = document.getElementById('lb-list');
  if (!list) return;

  var players = getLBPlayers();

  // Insert current user
  var myName = (currentUser && currentUser.username) ? currentUser.username : 'You';
  var me = { name:myName, coins:stormCoins, wins:_csSession ? _csSession.won : 0, played:_csSession ? _csSession.played : 0, avatar:myName[0].toUpperCase(), isMe:true };
  players.push(me);

  // Sort by tab
  players.sort(function(a,b){
    if (_lbTab==='coins')  return b.coins  - a.coins;
    if (_lbTab==='wins')   return b.wins   - a.wins;
    if (_lbTab==='played') return b.played - a.played;
    return 0;
  });

  var myRank = players.findIndex(function(p){ return p.isMe; }) + 1;
  var myEl   = document.getElementById('lb-my-rank');
  var myStatEl = document.getElementById('lb-my-stat');
  var myNameEl = document.getElementById('lb-my-name');
  var myAvatEl = document.getElementById('lb-my-avatar');
  if (myEl)   myEl.textContent   = '#' + myRank;
  if (myNameEl) myNameEl.textContent = myName;
  if (myAvatEl) myAvatEl.textContent = myName[0].toUpperCase();
  if (myStatEl) {
    if (_lbTab==='coins')  myStatEl.textContent = '⚡' + stormCoins.toLocaleString() + ' coins';
    if (_lbTab==='wins')   myStatEl.textContent = me.wins + ' casino wins';
    if (_lbTab==='played') myStatEl.textContent = me.played + ' games played';
  }

  var medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉'];
  var statFn = function(p) {
    if (_lbTab==='coins')  return '⚡' + p.coins.toLocaleString();
    if (_lbTab==='wins')   return '🏆 ' + p.wins + ' wins';
    if (_lbTab==='played') return '🎮 ' + p.played + ' played';
  };

  list.innerHTML = players.slice(0,15).map(function(p, i) {
    var rank  = i+1;
    var isTop = rank <= 3;
    var isMe  = !!p.isMe;
    var rankDisplay = isTop ? medals[rank-1] : ('<span style="font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:var(--muted);">#'+rank+'</span>');
    return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:14px;padding:12px 16px;border-radius:14px;margin-bottom:6px;transition:background 0.15s;'
      + (isMe  ? 'background:rgba(124,58,237,0.1);border:1px solid rgba(124,58,237,0.25);'
        : isTop ? 'background:rgba(245,158,11,0.04);border:1px solid rgba(245,158,11,0.1);'
        : 'background:rgba(255,255,255,0.02);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);')
      + '">'
      + '<div style="width:28px;text-align:center;flex-shrink:0;">' + rankDisplay + '</div>'
      + '<div style="width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:50%;flex-shrink:0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;'
      +   'background:' + (isMe ? 'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--accent),var(--accent2))' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)') + ';">'
      +   p.avatar
      + '</div>'
      + '<div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">'
      +   '<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;' + (isMe?'color:var(--accent2);':'') + '">' + p.name + (isMe?' 👈':'') + '</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:Rajdhani,sans-serif;font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:' + (isTop?'var(--coin)':'rgba(255,255,255,0.6)') + ';">'
      +   statFn(p)
      + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

// ── DOM READY — MASTER INIT ───────────────────────────────────
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
  restoreAccentColor();
  loadAchData();
  initNav();
  _discoverPlayers.init();
  showThemePickerIfNeeded();
  loadStreak();
  updateLevelUI();
  // Load saved avatar
  var savedAvatar = localStorage.getItem('gv_avatar');
  if (savedAvatar) applyAvatarToUI(savedAvatar);
  loadDC(); renderDC(); startChallengeTimer();
  initSpinWheel();
  fxInit();
  initNavRingCanvas();
  initWinsTicker();

  // ── DEFERRED FUNCTION PATCHES ────────────────────────────────

  var _origAddToLibrary = addToLibrary;
  addToLibrary = function(game, btn) {
    _origAddToLibrary(game, btn);
    if (typeof trackDC !== 'undefined') trackDC('lib_adds', 1);
  };

  var _origLaunchGame = launchGame;
  launchGame = async function(game) {
    await _origLaunchGame(game);
  };

  var _origUpdateCoins = updateCoins;
  updateCoins = function(delta) {
    _origUpdateCoins(delta);
    if (delta > 0) bumpCoins();
    if (delta >= 500) spawnCoinRain(12);
  };

  var _origAddLiveBet = addLiveBet;
  addLiveBet = function(user, game, amount, profit) {
    _origAddLiveBet(user, game, amount, profit);
    if (user === 'You' && profit >= 200) spawnCoinRain(profit >= 1000 ? 30 : 16);
  };

  var _origMakeCard = makeCard;
  makeCard = function(game, delay) {
    var card = _origMakeCard(game, delay);
    if (searchQuery) {
      var titleEl = card.querySelector('.card-title');
      if (titleEl) titleEl.innerHTML = highlightTitle(game.title, searchQuery);
    }
    return card;
  };

  if (!localStorage.getItem('gv_hints_shown')) {
    setTimeout(function() {
      showToast('Tip: Press 1–8 to switch tabs, / to search', { type: 't-info', icon: '⌨️', duration: 5000 });
      localStorage.setItem('gv_hints_shown', '1');
    }, 3000);
  }
});
