var THEMES = [
  { id:'purple',   name:'Default',  dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#6d28d9,#a855f7)', a:'#7c3aed', a2:'#a855f7', glow:'rgba(124,58,237,0.5)',  bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#0a0812,#13091f,#0a0812)' },
  { id:'blue',     name:'Midnight', dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#1d4ed8,#3b82f6)', a:'#2563eb', a2:'#60a5fa', glow:'rgba(37,99,235,0.5)',   bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#060a14,#0a1228,#060a14)' },
  { id:'green',    name:'Forest',   dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#065f46,#34d399)', a:'#059669', a2:'#34d399', glow:'rgba(5,150,105,0.5)',   bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#02100a,#051a10,#02100a)' },
  { id:'red',      name:'Crimson',  dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#991b1b,#f87171)', a:'#dc2626', a2:'#f87171', glow:'rgba(220,38,38,0.5)',   bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#110404,#1e0606,#110404)' },
  { id:'orange',   name:'Sunset',   dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#c2410c,#fb923c)', a:'#ea580c', a2:'#fb923c', glow:'rgba(234,88,12,0.5)',   bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#100802,#1c0f04,#100802)' },
  { id:'cyan',     name:'Ocean',    dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#0e7490,#22d3ee)', a:'#0891b2', a2:'#22d3ee', glow:'rgba(8,145,178,0.5)',   bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#020d10,#041820,#020d10)' },
  { id:'lavender', name:'Lavender', dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#7c3aed,#c4b5fd)', a:'#8b5cf6', a2:'#c4b5fd', glow:'rgba(139,92,246,0.45)', bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#0a0815,#14102a,#0a0815)' },
  { id:'mono',     name:'Mono',     dot:'linear-gradient(135deg,#374151,#9ca3af)', a:'#6b7280', a2:'#d1d5db', glow:'rgba(107,114,128,0.4)', bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,#080808,#111111,#080808)' },
];

function applyTheme(theme, save) {
  var r = document.documentElement.style;
  r.setProperty('--accent',        theme.a);
  r.setProperty('--accent2',       theme.a2);
  r.setProperty('--theme-accent',  theme.a);
  r.setProperty('--theme-accent2', theme.a2);
  r.setProperty('--theme-glow',    theme.glow);
  document.body.style.background = theme.bg;
  // Update the nav ring CSS var so conic-gradient repaints
  r.setProperty('--nav-ring-a',  theme.a);
  r.setProperty('--nav-ring-a2', theme.a2);
  if (save) {
    localStorage.setItem('gv_theme', theme.id);
    localStorage.setItem('gv_bg', 'theme');
  }
  // Re-position ring in case page reflowed
  if (typeof positionNavRing === 'function') setTimeout(positionNavRing, 50);
}

function buildOnboardingThemes() {
  var grid = document.getElementById('onboard-themes');
  if (!grid) return;
  var savedId = localStorage.getItem('gv_theme') || 'purple';
  grid.innerHTML = THEMES.map(function(t) {
    var sel = t.id === savedId;
    return '<div class="onboard-theme-card' + (sel ? ' selected' : '') + '" onclick="selectOnboardTheme(this,\'' + t.id + '\')">'
      + '<div class="onboard-theme-dot" style="background:' + t.dot + ';"></div>'
      + '<div class="onboard-theme-name">' + t.name + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
  var defaultTheme = THEMES.find(function(t){ return t.id === savedId; }) || THEMES[0];
  applyTheme(defaultTheme, false);
}

function selectOnboardTheme(el, themeId) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.onboard-theme-card').forEach(function(c){ c.classList.remove('selected'); });
  el.classList.add('selected');
  var theme = THEMES.find(function(t){ return t.id === themeId; });
  if (theme) applyTheme(theme, false);
}

// ── ONBOARDING AVATAR ────────────────────────────────────────
var _obSelectedAvatar = null; // emoji string or data:url

var OB_EMOJIS = ['😎','🔥','👑','⚡','🎮','🎯','🏆','💎',
                 '🐺','🦊','🐉','🦁','🤖','👾','💀','🌙',
                 '🎲','🃏','🌟','💜','🔮','🎭','🦋','❄️'];

function buildOnboardingAvatars() {
  var grid = document.getElementById('ob-emoji-grid');
  if (!grid) return;
  // Default select first
  if (!_obSelectedAvatar) { _obSelectedAvatar = OB_EMOJIS[0]; }
  grid.innerHTML = OB_EMOJIS.map(function(e) {
    var sel = _obSelectedAvatar === e;
    return '<div onclick="obSelectEmoji(\'' + e + '\')" style="'
      + 'width:100%;aspect-ratio:1;border-radius:10px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;'
      + 'font-size:18px;cursor:pointer;transition:all 0.15s;'
      + 'background:' + (sel ? 'rgba(139,92,246,0.25)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)') + ';'
      + 'border:1.5px solid ' + (sel ? 'rgba(139,92,246,0.7)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)') + ';'
      + '">' + e + '</div>';
  }).join('');
  updateObAvatarPreview();
}

function obSelectEmoji(e) {
  _obSelectedAvatar = e;
  buildOnboardingAvatars();
}

function obHandleImageUpload(input) {
  var file = input.files && input.files[0];
  if (!file) return;
  var reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = function(ev) {
    _obSelectedAvatar = ev.target.result; // data URL
    updateObAvatarPreview();
    // Deselect emoji grid
    var grid = document.getElementById('ob-emoji-grid');
    if (grid) grid.querySelectorAll('div').forEach(function(d){
      d.style.background = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)';
      d.style.borderColor = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)';
    });
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
}

function updateObAvatarPreview() {
  var preview = document.getElementById('ob-avatar-preview');
  if (!preview) return;
  if (_obSelectedAvatar && _obSelectedAvatar.startsWith('data:')) {
    preview.innerHTML = '<img src="' + _obSelectedAvatar + '" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;border-radius:16px;">';
    preview.style.padding = '0';
    preview.style.fontSize = '0';
  } else {
    preview.innerHTML = _obSelectedAvatar || '⚡';
    preview.style.padding = '';
    preview.style.fontSize = '';
  }
}

function applyAvatarToUI(avatarData) {
  // Apply to account button avatar
  var avatar = document.getElementById('account-avatar');
  var bigAvatar = document.getElementById('profile-big-avatar');
  [avatar, bigAvatar].forEach(function(el) {
    if (!el) return;
    if (avatarData && avatarData.startsWith('data:')) {
      el.innerHTML = '<img src="' + avatarData + '" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;border-radius:50%;">';
      el.style.fontSize = '0';
      el.style.padding = '0';
    } else if (avatarData) {
      el.textContent = avatarData;
      el.style.fontSize = '';
      el.style.padding = '';
    }
  });
}

function confirmOnboarding() {
  // Save avatar
  if (_obSelectedAvatar) {
    localStorage.setItem('gv_avatar', _obSelectedAvatar);
    applyAvatarToUI(_obSelectedAvatar);
  }
  var uInput = document.getElementById('onboard-username');
  var uVal = uInput ? uInput.value.trim() : '';
  if (uVal) {
    currentUser = { username: uVal, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
    localStorage.setItem('gv_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser));
    saveState();
    updateAccountBtn();
  }
  var sel = document.querySelector('.onboard-theme-card.selected');
  if (sel) {
    var onclick = sel.getAttribute('onclick') || '';
    var match = onclick.match(/selectOnboardTheme\(this,'([^']+)'\)/);
    if (match) {
      var theme = THEMES.find(function(t){ return t.id === match[1]; });
      if (theme) applyTheme(theme, true);
    }
  }
  _closeOnboarding();
}

function skipOnboarding() {
  if (!localStorage.getItem('gv_theme')) applyTheme(THEMES[0], true);
  _closeOnboarding();
}

function _closeOnboarding() {
  var overlay = document.getElementById('theme-picker-overlay');
  if (!overlay) return;
  overlay.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s ease';
  overlay.style.opacity = '0';
  setTimeout(function() { overlay.style.display = 'none'; overlay.style.opacity = ''; }, 320);
  sessionStorage.setItem('gv_session_started', '1');
  localStorage.setItem('gv_theme_chosen', '1');
}

function buildThemePicker() { buildOnboardingThemes(); }
function confirmTheme() { confirmOnboarding(); }

function openThemePicker() {
  buildOnboardingThemes();
  var overlay = document.getElementById('theme-picker-overlay');
  if (overlay) {
    overlay.style.opacity = '0';
    overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    overlay.style.transition = 'opacity 0.35s ease';
    setTimeout(function(){ overlay.style.opacity = '1'; }, 10);
  }
}

function buildSettingsThemeSwatches() {
  var grid = document.getElementById('settings-theme-swatches');
  if (!grid) return;
  var savedId = localStorage.getItem('gv_theme') || 'purple';
  grid.innerHTML = THEMES.map(function(t) {
    var active = t.id === savedId;
    return '<div onclick="quickApplyTheme(\'' + t.id + '\')" '
      + 'style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:5px;cursor:pointer;padding:8px 6px;border-radius:10px;'
      + 'border:1.5px solid ' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.07)') + ';'
      + 'background:' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)') + ';'
      + 'box-shadow:' + (active ? '0 0 12px ' + t.glow : 'none') + ';'
      + 'transition:all 0.2s;min-width:56px;">'
      + '<div style="width:24px;height:24px;border-radius:6px;background:' + t.dot + ';box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);"></div>'
      + '<span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:0.5px;text-transform:uppercase;color:' + (active ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.85)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)') + ';">' + t.name + '</span>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function quickApplyTheme(themeId) {
  var theme = THEMES.find(function(t){ return t.id === themeId; });
  if (!theme) return;
  applyTheme(theme, true);
  buildSettingsThemeSwatches();
  showToast('Theme: ' + theme.name, { type: 't-info', icon: '🎨' });
}

function selectThemeSwatch(el, themeId) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.theme-swatch').forEach(function(s){ s.classList.remove('selected'); });
  el.classList.add('selected');
  var theme = THEMES.find(function(t){ return t.id === themeId; });
  if (theme) applyTheme(theme, false);
}

function showThemePickerIfNeeded() {
  buildOnboardingThemes();
  buildOnboardingAvatars();
  var overlay = document.getElementById('theme-picker-overlay');
  if (overlay) {
    overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    overlay.style.animation = 'obIn 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.22,1,0.36,1) both';
  }
  var savedId = localStorage.getItem('gv_theme') || 'purple';
  var theme = THEMES.find(function(t){ return t.id === savedId; }) || THEMES[0];
  applyTheme(theme, false);
}

// ── NAV RING POSITIONING ──────────────────────────────────────
function positionNavRing() {
  var pill = document.querySelector('.topnav');
  var ring = document.getElementById('nav-border-ring');
  var glow = document.getElementById('nav-border-glow');
  if (!pill || !ring) return;
  var r = pill.getBoundingClientRect();
  var pad = 2;
  // Size the ring to exactly hug the pill
  ring.style.top    = (r.top    - pad) + 'px';
  ring.style.left   = (r.left   - pad) + 'px';
  ring.style.width  = (r.width  + pad * 2) + 'px';
  ring.style.height = (r.height + pad * 2) + 'px';
  // The ::before circle size must be large enough to reach corners
  // diagonal of the pill = sqrt(w^2 + h^2), use that as diameter
  var diag = Math.ceil(Math.sqrt(r.width * r.width + r.height * r.height)) + 20;
  var style = document.getElementById('nav-ring-style');
  if (!style) {
    style = document.createElement('style');
    style.id = 'nav-ring-style';
    document.head.appendChild(style);
  }
  style.textContent =
    '#nav-border-ring::before, #nav-border-glow::before {' +
    '  width:' + diag + 'px;height:' + diag + 'px;' +
    '  margin-top:-' + Math.ceil(diag/2) + 'px;' +
    '  margin-left:-' + Math.ceil(diag/2) + 'px;' +
    '}';
  if (glow) {
    glow.style.top    = (r.top    - pad) + 'px';
    glow.style.left   = (r.left   - pad) + 'px';
    glow.style.width  = (r.width  + pad * 2) + 'px';
    glow.style.height = (r.height + pad * 2) + 'px';
  }
}

// Position on load and on resize
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  // Multiple retries — pill needs time to render fully
  setTimeout(positionNavRing, 50);
  setTimeout(positionNavRing, 200);
  setTimeout(positionNavRing, 600);
  window.addEventListener('resize', positionNavRing);
});
</script>
